President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
The Path of Return  
All fallen human beings have fallen from their original position in creation, and we know that we must return to that original standard, that is, we must go back. This applies not only to individuals but also to families, tribes, nations, the world, and ultimately to heaven.  
The Destiny of the Path of Return  
When you think about the noun "return," you must consider it in relation to something greater. While it is important for oneself to be restored, we have the monumental task of restoring families beyond ourselves, tribes beyond families, nations beyond tribes, and ultimately returning to heaven.  
We must return to our original hometown. However, we must recognize that even if we carry the destiny to return to our hometown, centered on our individual selves, we cannot settle in that hometown. Up until now, our ancestors have sacrificed to find the original world they were meant to reach, but they have not fulfilled the mission of restoration. Therefore, our principles teach us that we must repeat the path of return.  
On March 14, 1970 (Saturday), at the Unification Industry Dormitory Auditorium (Sutaek-ri).  
* This speech was given at the 2nd Association Executive Training Session.  
The Path of Return  
We cannot avoid the issue of becoming sacrificial offerings and walking the path of return again. Even if my individual self returns to the hometown, I must find my family again, and that cannot be done by returning to the hometown. We must find our families in this lost land and return to the hometown. This is the fundamental meaning that our principles teach.  
For example, someone like Jacob had to leave his hometown to fulfill his purpose. He hoped to establish a happy family in the environment where his parents and relatives were, which was the desire of Jacob and all others. However, the one responsible for restoration, facing the path of return, cannot avoid that path. One cannot find a family in their hometown. In other words, unless one leaves their hometown and goes to the satanic world to find a family and returns, the path of return remains. This is why those who have taken responsibility on the path of restoration until now have had to walk that path. If one cannot physically walk that path, they must at least have the determination to do so mentally. Without that, one cannot return to God.  
Considering this issue, can you enjoy the happiness of your hometown while you are in the fallen realm? The answer is no. You must return to your hometown. You cannot return alone. Even if you return alone, you must find your family again, and even if your family returns, you must find your tribe again. Even if the tribe returns, you must find your nation again. You cannot find your nation in your hometown either. You must go back to the satanic world and fight to find your nation, and unless you achieve victory, your nation cannot return to the hometown. You must understand this. Furthermore, even if a nation returns to the hometown, that nation must establish its sovereignty and lay a victorious foundation against the sovereignty of the satanic world, and must confront the satanic nations again. This is unavoidable. Even if a nation is established, that alone does not end the path of return; because the world exists, there remains the destiny to save the world and return.  
For this reason, even Jesus, after living for over 30 years on this earth and facing death, did not end his mission. When Jesus said, "It is finished" just before his death, he meant that he had reached the position to go to the Father. It was not that he was going with all his hopes fulfilled; rather, it was a statement that he was walking the path of suffering that he had to go through. Therefore, even though he left such words, Jesus had to fight to find the internal and spiritual foundation that needed to be established on earth during the 40 days after his resurrection. Only after establishing this foundation can the path to return spiritually be opened.  
Although Jesus returned spiritually, he was not in a position to rest in the embrace of God. He had to come back to earth and fight to develop the family, tribal, national, and world forms centered on Christianity. Thus, we know that Jesus had to take responsibility and come forward in the search for the hometown. From this perspective, when we think about ourselves on the path to the hometown we must return to today, we are in the same position. Just like countless prophets returned, the path we must walk today is the same.  
The Mission of the Unification Church  
So what has humanity sought until now? An ideal world, that is, utopia. Humanity has pursued such a world, but that world is not before us. Instead of presenting conditions for happiness, we are faced with conditions of unhappiness and despair. We are hitting a wall. So what should we do here? We must return. Because there is a future goal, we are in a position where we must turn back from the path of life we have been walking and seek another path.  
Considering this, our Unification Church today, and the world of humanity, presents the path to the hometown we must return to. Will it be enough for us to return alone? No. Even if we return, we will again be placed in a destiny that requires us to come back. Therefore, God has a strategy: before returning, He sends His people, the people of the hometown. That is why He has worked hard until now.  
What about the countless prophets and ancestors who have taken on the responsibility of restoration on this earth? They are in a position similar to those who have left their hometown to live in a foreign land. Who are the people that God has sent? They are not prodigals. He has sent those who are in a position of filial piety. He has sent filial sons and daughters to save those who are unfilial like prodigals on this earth. Through those filial children, He has been working to gather one brotherhood, one tribe, one nation, and one country throughout the long history of 6,000 years.  
God has sent His beloved sons and daughters to establish an absolute nation, but at this point, has He prepared the foundation to restore one nation? No, He has not. Due to repeated failures, He has sent heavenly people to manage, promote, and accomplish that work on this earth, which is the history of heaven until now.  
From this perspective, God has established the Unification Church on this earth today. In what position has He established it? Not on the foundation of heaven, but in the satanic world. It has been established in a place swarming with prodigals. In other words, we are not in the position of filial children living comfortably and being loved in our hometown; we are in a position where we must go to the place where prodigals live, leaving our parents and relatives behind, to save our brothers, tribes, and return. This applies not only to the Unification Church but to all religions sent by God; they are all in a position of living in a foreign land.  
Therefore, we must always return to our hometown. The more difficult the foreign life is, the more we should long for the day we can return to our hometown. However, we cannot return alone. The reason I have been sent to this earth is not because my individual self is needed. Therefore, I must inevitably lead my family, tribe, nation, and country. If I do not, the path to my hometown itself will become a path of sorrow, and you must understand this.  
What was the purpose of Jesus coming to this earth and spending over 30 years fighting? It was to enter the path of return to the hometown centered on the nation of Israel. He fought to lead the nation and fulfill that work, but he failed. When we think of the sorrowful path of that failure being the path of the cross, what should the Christians who emerged from that sorrowful foundation do? They must pursue the path to return to the hometown by welcoming the Lord who will come again on the foundation of a nation. This has been the history of Christianity until now. This is a historical desire and the purpose of the struggle that Jesus himself has been engaged in for 2,000 years, connecting with the Holy Spirit and serving God centered on the earth.  
So what position does the Unification Church hold? We are in a position where we must find and establish heavenly individuals, heavenly families, heavenly tribes, heavenly nations, and heavenly countries in this satanic world, taking on the responsibility to return to the hometown. Therefore, each individual in the Unification Church has the responsibility to gather families, tribes, and nations that can return to the hometown. This is the mission that the Unification Church bears today.  
What position do Unification Church members hold?  
Until now, humans have seen God from the position of fallen beings, believing that God exists in glory without suffering or pain. Many religions have understood and practiced their faith in this way throughout history. However, when we truly understand God, what position is He in? God is in the position of having lost His family, His children, all His possessions, His nation, and the world. The one who is in such a position is our Father. When we meet that Father, we believe that all our grievances will be resolved, and everything we have longed for will be fulfilled. However, when we come to find this path and meet our parents, we realize that not only their possessions but everything in the world is in the hands of the enemy.  
Knowing this, we have the responsibility to liberate those parents. Furthermore, we must find the original nation that the parents of humanity should have, so we must make a resolution. Since we cannot find that in our hometown, we are destined to go toward the place that the satanic world has taken away. This is the position we are in as we trace the path of restoration. Until now, we have established religions to seek the path to the hometown, but when we arrive at that place and meet our Father, we will not be welcomed and comforted with joy; rather, we will realize that we have a collective responsibility to find His family, tribe, nation, and country.  
Because God is in such a position, He has been blocking humanity from coming close to Him. He has built barriers to prevent us from approaching Him until now. Although He desperately wants to reveal all His circumstances to humanity, He is in a position where He cannot do so. Because of this position, does He not want to sacrifice countless people who have overcome the path of suffering and hardship? Therefore, God has never communicated His circumstances to humanity throughout history. You must understand that this is rather a manifestation of His love for humanity.  
Many people have started for the purpose of His will in this world, but none have known the circumstances of such a Father. In this position, the Unification Church has conveyed and taught the position of that Father, and you must feel that this is a position that carries the entire mission and hope of the Father and the life and death issues of the Unification Church. The reason that the secrets of heaven have not been taught until now is not because the Father lacks love for humanity; we must understand that it is because of the unavoidable position He is in. If today we have been taught such internal matters, we will bear a double or triple responsibility.  
So what must we do now? When we come to know the Father, we realize that He is a pitiful being. The Father has lost His most beloved sons and daughters, and He has lost all the nations, countries, and worlds He should have governed. We realize that the Father is in such a position. So who caused the Father to be like this? The enemy. Then where is the enemy? We must go and confront the enemy and subdue them. We are in a position where we must annihilate that enemy and resolve the grievances that the parents have carried until now. You must understand that today’s Unification Church members are in such a position. You may have come to the path of restoration thinking it is good, but it is not just good; you must bear double and triple responsibilities.  
In the past, someone like Abraham received the command from God to leave Ur of the Chaldeans and left his hometown, but today, knowing the circumstances of the Father, we cannot help but leave our hometown even if God tells us not to. This is the position of today’s Unification Church members.
We are in a position to walk the path that historical prophets or our historical ancestors could not take, and that is why our historical ancestors are looking at us with hope. We must understand that they are looking at us with a second expectation, as a standard of hope.

Abraham left Ur of the Chaldeans upon receiving God's command, but now we recognize that we cannot go toward the world of Satan, and that step we have taken is the first step in the historical age. Therefore, we cannot help but regard Abraham as a being of hope.

Until now, countless prophets have sought to return to God, but there has been no one who started from the same position. No one has known God's situation and rushed to the battlefield. Therefore, you must understand that the fact that you are in such a position of responsibility is a historical event.

Now we have come to know the existence of our parents, and we have understood the tragedies of our nation up to this point. We have also come to know that the nation has perished. Who is to blame for this? It is not because of the mistakes of the parents. It is not because of the mistakes of the siblings. It is not because of the mistakes of the country or the nation that the father can govern. This mistake has been entirely caused by the enemy. In order to fulfill the duty of filial piety to our parents, we must not remain idle. If we understand this, we have the responsibility to repay this enemy. We must walk the path of struggle to repay the enemies of our parents, the enemies of our siblings, and the enemies of our kin and nation. No matter what suffering and pain we encounter on that path, we have the mission to overcome it without question.

One cannot resolve the sorrow of restoration without laying down their life. Today, you may think that if you are restored, everything will be over, but you must go before the Father from the position of being restored alone. The Father will certainly ask, "Did you come alone? What about your family? What about your tribe? What about your nation? What about your country?" And you will inevitably be sent back to this land. In order to meet a joyful day, if you do not establish your face and dignity before the Father, you will not be able to leave your hometown again. Knowing this fact, we must realize that we have responsibilities to fulfill before embarking on the path of returning home.

What did Jesus seek on this earth? Jesus came to this land centered on the purpose of national restoration. Before stepping toward Judaism, which could represent the nation, the foundation for restoring the tribe was the issue, and the problem was finding the relative conditions under which an individual could stand to restore the family. Here, the standard for individuals to come is established; when individuals are restored, they must find their families, and when families are restored, they must find their tribes. Furthermore, when tribes are restored, they must find their nations, and when nations are restored, they must find their countries. We must understand that without establishing a form of this country, we cannot inherit the Father's nation.

From this perspective, Jesus set that as a standard and walked the path of labor and effort for over thirty years, but all paths were blocked, so he had to transcend the historical environment to restore the nation centered on the spirit world. God, who knows this, could not help but allow the way of the cross. You must understand how miserable that position was. The suffering and trials that Jesus bore while carrying the cross to save humanity are bound up in the path of restoration today. Therefore, without having the heart to overcome this, one cannot be a responsible person on the path of restoration and returning home. Also, without such a heart, one cannot restore the family centered on oneself, cannot restore the tribe centered on the family, and cannot restore the nation centered on the tribe.

From this viewpoint, our responsibility today is not completed by simply being in the spirit world. We must live in fear of the day when we will go to the spirit world before returning home. We must place our lives on the line to deal with how to handle these issues throughout our lives, saving every hour, minute, and second to lay the foundation for such a life. Otherwise, we cannot establish our face before the Father, who has worked hard to find that nation until now, nor can we establish our face before the Father, who wishes to find the world. Being in this position is what it means to be a Unification Church member today.

When you wake up from sleep, you should feel that you are surrounded by the enemy's stronghold. The place where you are sleeping is not a place of rest, nor is it a place where you can eat and relax without worry. The issue is how to break through this environment surrounded by the enemy. You must not sleep in that place without establishing a defensive line for battle. You must also establish a defensive line in the environment where you act. Because you cannot bear this mission alone, the issue of gathering comrades arises.

The spies infiltrated by the North Korean puppet group are seriously active in this land. You must not have the same level of heart as them. You cannot restore without having a heart centered on God that is above that. To find the sovereignty of the world of Satan, you must risk your life, and on the path of restoring this world and taking responsibility for the destiny of the universe, you must lay down your life. Without doing so, you cannot resolve the sorrow you carry on the path of restoration. Therefore, you must be determined to lay down your life and resolve the sorrow you carry on the path of restoration.

To establish your face before God and the Teacher, until now you may have thought that if you did this much, everything would be fine. However, even though you have met the Teacher today, there is a distance between you and the Teacher. If you thought that meeting your parents would resolve everything, that would be a great misunderstanding. Just as God has such responsibilities, the Teacher is also bearing responsibilities that must be fulfilled on earth. You must not stand in the position of a prodigal son who returns in rags, having given up everything. You must be in the position of a filial son whom God desires, seeking the enemy to restore your children and returning with your possessions, like Jacob. Otherwise, you must understand that you cannot establish your face before God and cannot receive blessings when you return home.

It is good that you have come into the Unification Church and are looking at the Teacher in the midst of difficulties, trusting and following him. However, that is not the end. Up to this point, many religious people throughout history have pursued God as the object of their faith, believing that if they welcomed God, everything would go smoothly and be resolved, but in reality, when they went to the spirit world, it was not so. They must return to the earth and lay the foundation for cooperation. They must take on the mission of establishing a national foundation, a state foundation, and a global foundation and engage in the history of struggle again on the earth. In the same way, meeting your parents on earth does not mean that everything is over. From that point, a new struggle must begin.

When you meet your parents, you will find that they are not people who sing songs of happiness and live peacefully on this earth; rather, they are bearing the responsibility to find the nation and the world. They are not teaching about tomorrow's happiness but are in a position to teach about struggle. If there is an individual who thinks of finding a place of comfort and rest in light of such parents, it would be the greatest disloyalty. You must understand that it would be a double disloyalty. Those parents have families, tribes, nations, and the world that must be found. You must find those families, nations, and the world. You are in that position. If each of you fulfills this responsibility and mission, the nation will automatically be restored. The fact that you have become a blessed family is a blessing granted due to the efforts of heaven. Heaven does not give such blessings for you to simply inherit them and enjoy happiness in that place. You must understand that you are blessed to bear the responsibility of finding the tribe.

If there is a village that can bring the entire populace before the Unification Church, you must transcend your village to fulfill the responsibility for the district, county, and province. You must understand that if God has worked hard to find this, you cannot find the district, county, and province without making even greater efforts.

When we look at the Unification Church today, how strong is the support that God is providing behind the Unification Church? At this time, how much is God cooperating with the Unification Church? You must have the heart to make even greater efforts based on the degree of that cooperation. Thus, you must understand that you cannot lay the foundation for restoring the nation and state without standing in a position of actually working in such an environment. If you do not fulfill this task and go to the spirit world, what will happen? You will have to return to the earth.

The mission of Jesus, who came to this earth as the son of God, was to subdue numerous enemy nations centered on the nation of Israel. If that nation had become completely one with God, the nations of the world would have to submit. So how do we restore this Republic of Korea today? How do we restore this nation and people? Even if we say we have restored the southern land, how do we restore the north? That is the issue.

Today, the Unification Church itself must offer sacrifices from a national perspective to restore the nation. The Unification Church is in the position of Abel. Those who are in a national position are in the position of Cain, while the Unification Church is in the position of Abel. Is it not the principle's teaching that Abel cannot return without finding Cain? Does not the concept of substantial expectation speak to this? Abel alone cannot return. Abel alone cannot return as an individual. Abel's family alone cannot return. We must find the Cain-like individuals, the Cain-like families, the Cain-like tribes, the Cain-like nations, and the Cain-like countries. From this perspective, the division of the Republic of Korea into North and South is not a factor that brings us happiness. If another country other than ours were divided, how would we find that country? You must think about these issues.

Let us examine the division of the 38th parallel from the perspective of providence. Looking at the 38th parallel, God is watching over it.
I hope that soon the land of South Korea will be unified centered around your sons and daughters, becoming the Abel position of the Republic of Korea, and that it will subdue the Cain position of North Korea. When the land of South Korea is fully armed with ideology and all realities and becomes completely one, restoring the land of Cain will not be a problem. If that happens, wouldn't the central nation in Asia be automatically determined? From this perspective, we must be grateful for all the suffering that the Unification Church bears today. We are walking the destined path that this nation and this world must take. Each of us must understand this and be grateful for the suffering that we, as members of the Unification Church, must endure. Thus, one person gathers another, making two people, and two people gather to make four... By multiplying in this way, each of them must restore their own tribes and simultaneously expand that tribe into a national front to create one nation and restore the country. Isn't this the path that the Unification Church must take today? 

Our Unification Church currently bears the responsibility of restoring the nation, placing the people before us, the Republic of Korea. Therefore, today, the families of the teacher and your families must unite to form a unified tribe. In order to form a unified nation, you must take responsibility for three or more tribes. Since we must restore the lineage, whether it be Kim, Park, or Lee, the issue becomes how to develop ways to restore these three tribes. This is why the teacher blessed 430 couples and told them to become tribal messiahs.

The path that the Unification Church must take toward its homeland
Now, you must unite centered around the teacher's family, both inside and out. In doing so, you must not insert yourselves. You must go together with the goal and direction that the teacher's family aims for. When the commander gives the final attack order, the commander should not lead the way. The soldiers must run ahead of the commander; only then will the battle be victorious. If the commander steps forward and is the first to fall, the army will lose its direction. Here, what you must understand is that your families must unite like a fortress centered around the teacher's family. The members of the Unification Church must unite like a fortress centered around the teacher. Thus, the united group must march straight toward the front line.

We have taken on the solemn task of national restoration from the Abel position. This is a once-in-a-lifetime event in the history of restoration providence. It has never happened before. Because Jesus could not do this, we are fighting on this land for national restoration, equipped with the historical environment of today. You must understand that the fact that we first had this connection gives us the qualification to restore today.

Therefore, you must think about how to restore this nation, the Republic of Korea, whether it be how to restore South Korea or how to restore North Korea. It is not an external world issue. Even if North and South Korea are unified in the future, how will we educate the young people who grew up in North Korea after liberation? They are completely indoctrinated. How will we evangelize them? How will we educate them so that they can stand on our side and fight against the Chinese Communist Party or the Soviet Communist Party? In other words, how can we make them fight responsibly from the position of Cain, who has surrendered before Abel? Only by doing so can the Korean Peninsula be unified. Only then can North and South Korea finally unify, and the Korean people can finally resolve their historical grievances and stand before heaven as one sovereign nation, and again appear before the world. You must understand that this destined path remains. This is the path that the Unification Church must take today.

Now we have come to know the reality of our homeland very well. Upon hearing the news, I found that the homeland was an unhappy place. When I left my parents, I resolved to return after avenging them, so I must return having reclaimed something from the enemy's world. Thus, I have a responsibility to offer it before my parents. However, I must not return in a miserable state that is contrary to what I resolved to do when I left, causing my parents to weep again and becoming a pitiful figure who receives sympathy. To avoid that, I must fight even if it means death. I must be prepared to fight, even if it means collapsing somewhere. You must understand that the path to the homeland cannot be traveled without the willingness to face death.

That is why Jesus also said, "Abba Father, if it is possible, please allow me to fulfill this mission. But not my will, but Yours be done." Jesus knew that he could not find the Father's will without going through death. He followed the will until he crossed the hill of death. That was the path that Jesus took. It is also the traditional thought of Christianity. Because such traditional thought has continued, we too are faced with such a destiny today.

Therefore, the more we put blessed families on the front lines, the more they suffer, and the more they are hit, the faster they will be restored. If one family sacrifices, it can restore that neighborhood. When a family sacrifices, the environment for restoration to heaven increases more than when an individual sacrifices. From this perspective, putting blessed families on the path of suffering is God's love and a shortcut to saving the nation. However, if you cannot endure that suffering, how can you show your face in the world of the homeland?

Then what is the responsibility imposed on the Korean people today? It is to unify North and South Korea. Every time you sing the song of unification, you must remember this. And the Unification Church must be in the position of Abel in the land of South Korea. Abel must become the offering. It must not be about hitting and taking; it must be about standing firm and taking it out. We are not restoring based on the suffering we have endured so far. We are restoring based on results. We must present a condition that can awaken the conscience of the masses to achieve restoration. A good person suffering an unjust position allows those who know to be motivated, step by step restoring to where we are now.

Everyone, when we look at the Republic of Korea centered around this 70s, the enemy that has been treating us as Satan and enemies has now changed its position and is standing on equal footing with us, allowing us to have hope on our side. You must recognize that this is the time when this nation can survive and bring new liberation to this nation. From the time we crossed this boundary, we must set the standard of the nation and engage in fierce battles. Even if we are advancing toward the enemy, we must not be relieved just because the enemy does not resist. The less they resist, the more we must advance our command to push forward in this 70s.

The question is how to restore the Republic of Korea as quickly as possible.
Once we restore the Republic of Korea to heaven's side, then the enemies will all come together. When that happens, uniting thirty million people will be simple. Therefore, we must restore subjectivity. South Korea must seek the Cain-like nation from the Abel position. Because it is our destiny to unify what was divided between the Northern Kingdom of Israel and the Southern Kingdom of Judah, the division of South and North Korea is a providential conclusion for the Republic of Korea, which has taken on the responsibility on the path of restoration. Therefore, we must either shed blood in this fierce battle, die, or perish; one of these three must happen. Even if we perish, it is okay for just one of us to perish, but if I perish, the nation that can save countless descendants will perish. If that nation perishes, the world will perish.

That is why we cannot allow the world to perish, nor can we allow the nation to perish. The nation must not perish, and the Unification Church must not perish. The day you perish, the Unification Church will perish before the Communist Party. If that happens, we will not be able to achieve all the restoration we dreamed of in the Republic of Korea. If that happens, we will have to choose another country and fight to divide the sovereignty of that country again. Through which country can we rebuild such a foundation? It must be our thirty million people. Therefore, we must understand that our position is one that no one can slander.

Because the path of destiny that must bear responsibility for the nation and the people is the path of restoration, God has been looking at the last time left in the 6,000 years of historical providence and has been reclaiming until now. How do we overcome and surpass this critical moment of the Republic of Korea that remains at the end? When I look at the corruption of this country, I feel that I must seek solutions without being able to sleep at night. Seeing the miserable state of the environment, we must have confidence that we can win in tomorrow's battlefield, burning with righteous indignation. When we cross the front line, the Communist Party will perish. When that happens, Kim Il-sung of North Korea will not be the problem. The problem lies here.

Today, the teacher's position in seeking the path home is like this. The teacher left the homeland and came down to South Korea, seeking you until now. Even though there are beloved brothers, he has not been able to speak of his story before them. Because God has been in a position where He could not speak for the past 6,000 years of restoration history, the teacher also cannot speak. He could not speak even before beloved relatives and parents. Until now, there has been no one with whom God could speak. Therefore, to fulfill the mission of restoration, we must go into the enemy's world and give good things on behalf of that position. We must give with a heart greater than that which we had before our parents and family. In other words, we must be sincere for Cain. Without returning to Cain, there can be no Abel's family. There can be no family. A family can only be born from parents. A family cannot be born without parents.

If you want to have a happy family with your parents, you must have a lineage. Once the lineage has the environment to be happy, your family can serve your parents and rest. That lineage must take on the responsibility of fighting on behalf of the family. Who will defend the front line? Who will defend the front line? Today, there are no Abel-like beings in the Republic of Korea to defend the front line. But has there been a Cain-like being who has laid down the national and ethnic foundations to take responsibility for that front line? No, they have not. Therefore, you must take responsibility for this fight. If we lose this fight, the Unification Church and you will perish.

Kim Il-sung in the North is now looking at South Korea with the slogan of communist unification, fortifying both inside and out. What will happen if we cannot take responsibility here? Let us think. Currently, there is no way to save Korea as the Republic of Korea. Where is the way to save it? Looking at the situation in Asia, Korea is surrounded. There will be cases where Japan will provoke us. Isn't Japan currently engaging in behind-the-scenes negotiations, even able to hold political talks with China? From this perspective, our path seems vague.

In light of this urgent environment, what should we do? We must focus on the question of how to restore the Republic of Korea as quickly as possible in the face of this urgent situation. Thus, when Cain and Abel become one and stand before their parents, the lineage will be restored, and the Communist Party will not be a problem. Once the foundation for uniting the Republic of Korea centered around our ideology is laid, restoring the land of North Korea will not be a problem. <Words> We know well that the term "restoration" arose from the fall. Humanity lost the Creator who made us due to the fall. By losing that Creator, humans lost their true parents, and as a result of losing true parents, they lost true siblings, families, nations, and the world. In this way, we have lost everything that is considered most precious as human beings. 

So, what is it that we need to seek? We must not pursue our own glory or try to fulfill our own purposes. We need to find what is fundamental and most important to us. We must recognize that we need to fulfill purposes that can benefit this country and this world, rather than just our individual purposes.

True Hopes of Humanity
Looking at our Republic of Korea, it is currently divided into two countries. The North and the South are separated by the 38th parallel. From this dual perspective, what do we desire? We wish to return to the state before the division. In other words, we want to become one. This is undoubtedly a common hope of the people living in this nation, whether in the North or the South.

However, even if the North and South were to unify, meaning that the wishes of the nation are fulfilled and reconciliation is achieved, that would not be the end. No matter how unified the North and South become, if the world is not unified, we must work towards unifying the world as well. In other words, we must either stand in the position of the subject or the object. If we do not do so, even if we become a unified nation, we will not be able to advance towards the future with hope for the world.

Furthermore, even if we say we have made the world one centered around the Republic of Korea, that is not the end. We know that there is not only the physical world but also an inner world. In other words, while there is a terrestrial world, there is also a celestial world. Therefore, even if we have made the world one, what we pursue next is the unification of the intangible world and the tangible world.

So, does it end just because we have made the tangible world and the intangible world one? No. Even if we have made heaven and earth, or in the terminology of the Unification Church, the cosmos one, unless we have the central being who is the master, we cannot stand in a position where a unified nation, a unified world, or a unified cosmos can be integrated with that central being. In other words, since all creation is a being that has been created, unless it stands in a position of unity with the central being that created it, and unless a perfect central being and a perfect counterpart are determined, the ultimate world we desire cannot manifest.

Therefore, when we become the eternal counterparts of that central being and are in a position to fulfill something greater, we cannot help but think that we will finally establish a relationship with God.

Throughout the long historical process until now, what was the desire of the countless people who have taken on the mission of the restoration providence? It was for the individual to become one with heaven. After that, the standard of this desire must be expanded to the family becoming one with God. However, even if the family becomes one, that is not the end. After becoming the absolute central counterpart, one must face the issue of leading one’s tribe to unite with the eternal center.

We know that the family that stood in such a position was the family of Jacob. The family of Jacob includes Jacob's parents, Jacob's siblings, and Jacob's children. God raised Jacob's tribe to establish a national form centered on Jacob and his relatives of over 70 people.

This was because without establishing a relationship between Jacob, who could become one with the absolute God, the family that could become one with Jacob, and the tribe that could become one with the family, it would not be possible to set a standard to unify the nation. Therefore, God's purpose in finding and establishing individuals is to establish families, and the purpose in establishing families is to establish tribes, and the purpose in establishing tribes is to establish nations, and the purpose in establishing nations is to establish the victorious nation of Israel. We understand well this history of God's providence.

The nation that has the authority to represent the kingdom of heaven on earth is the nation of Israel, and the people of Israel stand in the position of the chosen people who have been selected by God to represent all humanity. These two must become one. For them to become one, they must be united around the territory, and for that, the territory must not be divided. The land must become one, and the people must become a harmonious people. Thus, a sovereign nation that can become one with God must be established. For this reason, God has been carrying out the restoration providence for 4,000 years. We know that what He aimed to achieve through this was the first nation of Israel. Although Israel hoped to bring the whole world under its control, we must understand that such a thing did not happen due to the providential content, and thus the nation of Israel disappeared from the earth.

The Mission of Jesus
Then, what should Jesus, who came as a substitute for the nation of Israel, have done? He had to become one with God from the position where the sovereignty of Israel, the people of Israel, and the land of Israel were unified. Even if Jesus stood in the position of leading the nation of Israel, that alone was not enough. Next, he needed to establish a foundation based on principles to prepare a victorious ground without having to confront a Cain-like nation. This was Jesus' position. We must understand that this was the mission of Jesus sent to this earth.

The maintenance of a nation cannot be achieved by that nation alone. A nation facing a great enemy cannot sustain itself by its own strength. For a nation to be maintained, it must cooperate with neighboring nations. It must become one with neighboring nations. The development of a nation also requires a form of union.

The same goes for establishing the heavenly world. No matter how Abel-like Israel has established its national standards, it cannot return without subjugating the Cain-like national authority. In other words, to appear as parents on this earth, Cain and Abel must become one in the family of Adam. Without the reconciliation of Cain and Abel, parents cannot be restored. To restore parents, it cannot be done by Abel alone. Abel must lead Cain in order to achieve restoration according to the principle.

For this reason, Jesus, who came to the Abel-like nation of Israel, must subjugate the Cain-like nations. The greater the nation he subjugates, the faster the world will be restored. This has been the principle by which God has been restoring until now. So, what was the greatest Cain-like nation before the nation of Israel? It was the Roman Empire. How could Jesus subjugate this Roman Empire? If Jesus had governed the nation of Israel and simultaneously subjugated the Roman Empire, the world would have been opened up for immediate subjugation, but if he could not subjugate it, a global struggle would remain on the path of restoration.

However, because the nation of Israel could not do this centered on Jesus, he had to fight against the global enemies wherever he went and could not avoid crossing that hurdle. Therefore, the path of Christianity has been a path that requires the willingness to face death. You must understand this.

Abel Must Give Everything to Cain
The title of today's message is the "Restoration Point." What does this restoration point mean? Even if Israel became a nation capable of restoring the world, that nation alone is not enough. You are likely aware of the restoration era of the substance of Cain and Abel through the principles, that is, the era of substance. Similarly, centered on the nation of Israel, we must subjugate the Cain-like nations, that is, the archangel-type nations. This is not done through force. Since Abel was killed by his older brother Cain, one must enter into the position of death, that is, the position of being struck, and without having the conditions to live and subjugate them, the restoration point cannot appear.

For this reason, Jacob wanted to offer all his possessions and his servant, found after 21 years of labor, before his brother Esau. Jacob said, "My life and my possessions belong to my brother," and as he presented all his wealth to Esau, Esau accepted all of Jacob's possessions. Receiving the gifts meant accepting Jacob, and accepting Jacob meant accepting Jacob's family, and accepting the family meant accepting the nation of Israel, and accepting the nation of Israel meant being able to accept the nation of Israel itself.

In other words, it is about giving everything to Cain and then asking for it back. This is the principle of restoration. The positions of God and Satan are the positions of Abel and Cain. Therefore, God has given everything to Satan until now. He has given individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world. He has given everything.

He has said, "Do as you please with the world." He has given everything to the point where even God can be denied, to the point where one could say God is dead. He has given everything. Therefore, He has been completely denied. What does this fact appearing in history mean? It means that behind the complete denial, the emergence of complete affirmation is inherent.

The positions of traitors and loyalists are the same. For a loyalist to have the authority of a loyalist, they must stand in a position of complete denial. Only then can they participate in the ranks of loyalists that can be revealed in the historical process. Similarly, Jesus had to walk a path of such a destiny. He had to be completely denied. By whom? In front of the world of Satan. So, what does it mean to be denied? It means to give everything up. However, if one were to treat them as enemies or attack them, it would lead to destruction. There would be no way to return.

For this reason, what did Jesus pray while hanging on the cross? "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do." (Luke 23:34) This place of "forgive them" is the position of giving all of one’s possessions to the enemy. Even if one does not want to, they will have to give it up.

All the precious things brought from heaven, the nation of Israel established through the sacrifices of 4,000 years, seeing it about to be taken away, Jesus was filled with extreme indignation and resentment, but he still said, "Forgive them their sins." This was a strategy to seek a way to give everything to the enemy and then reclaim it. If their sins are not forgiven, there will be no way for the things that have been handed over to Satan to return. Without opening a way for them to be forgiven, we will completely lose the nation of Israel that has been established through all that labor. We will not be able to find the restoration point.

For this reason, even though Jesus was in a miserable position, he prayed for his enemies. This fact became a motive that could completely subjugate the connections of the two worlds. One is God, who, having lost His original authority, cannot love the enemy, but has opened a way to love, and the other is the enemies who, having no choice but to perish, have had a way opened for their revival. We must understand that this is where Christianity has developed.

The Path of Self-Denial
From this perspective, if the path of the Unification Church today is the right path, then our path is the same as that time. Just as God stood in a position to reclaim everything that was taken away by the enemy, the path of the Unification Church today is the same. It would be good if our Unification Church were welcomed by this country and this nation, but if that happens, it will be in a position to accept the things of the world of Satan as they are. Therefore, there must be a denial that takes place.

Either Abel must deny Cain, or Cain must deny Abel; one of the two must be denied. What does this mean? It means that no matter how welcomed the Unification Church is by a nation, it cannot simply love that nation as it is. In order to love, one must go to another nation and come back with the conditions to be welcomed, and only then can one love the people of that nation. Therefore, that nation cannot take a position of simply being welcomed. Because it has not been welcomed, that is, because it has faced opposition, when viewed from the restoration point, it can stand closer to God and can establish a historical connection of restoration on this earth.

What has the history of the past looked like from this standpoint? It has been a miserable history in itself. It has been a history of losing everything. Ultimately, it must be lost. Otherwise, it will be taken away. It must be given. Just as God has handed everything over to Satan, we too must hand everything over. From such a position, we must establish a standard that says we have completely reclaimed it. Here, a new connection for restoration is formed. Thus, restoring based on this original posture is the path of restoration destiny, and therefore, the path we must take today inevitably cannot avoid the path of suffering. This is a very reasonable logic.

So, what should we do? We must deny ourselves. Who should we deny ourselves for? We must deny ourselves for the sake of finding this nation. 

If Jesus had forcibly given up his life, he would not have been able to become the Savior. Of course, Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, "Abba, Father, all things are possible for You; take this cup away from Me; nevertheless, not what I will, but what You will." (Mark 14:36) By overcoming the path of ultimate death centered on the Father’s will, the issue changed from there.

He denied himself. He was not sacrificed by force but voluntarily sacrificed himself. One must not be sacrificed by force but must sacrifice oneself voluntarily. Abel was not voluntarily sacrificed before Cain; he was forcibly sacrificed. The place where Abel was sacrificed could not be a place of joy; it was a place of sorrow, which is why the issue of restoration follows.

Therefore, restoration cannot be forced. One must deny oneself. In any era, or even in the world of Satan, which is outside of God's providential authority, history is directed by those who walk this path. Conscientious people, good people, those who are rejected by the masses for no reason, and even those who have authority...
without cutting off the relationship with Satan. You must cut off that relationship to return to the original position. 

The point of restoration is ourselves. From a principled perspective, how did Adam and Eve fall? They fell because they did not trust God. Therefore, they could not become the embodiment of what God desired. That is the fall. Who caused them to distrust? It was Satan. Why could they not become the embodiment of God? Because Satan held them captive. Why could they not have the opportunity for eternal love? Because of deceptive love centered on Satan. Because you are in this position, you must cut off Satan.

Therefore, regardless of your social status or class, whether you are a university professor with authority or a sovereign of a nation, you cannot retain that authority without severing the relationship with Satan. You must cut off that relationship to return to the original position. 

You must understand that the restoration path is not just about external circumstances but about internal transformation. The internal must be dealt with first before the external can be addressed. The internal issues revolve around emotional connections centered on oneself. This includes relationships with siblings. Wouldn’t it be wonderful if we could just hold onto our siblings and restore everything? But that is not possible. Wouldn’t it be great if we could just hold onto our parents and restore everything? But that is not possible. What about holding onto our beloved spouse? That too is not possible. If we could just hold onto everything we possess and restore it, how wonderful would that be? But that is not possible either. This is the crux of the issue.

We must let go of both the external and internal. If we do not let go, we will inevitably lose everything. If we do not, God cannot work. We must either let go or be taken away. Abel stood in a position that was not chosen by himself, yet because he was in a position of being taken away, God was on his side.

Today, we are in such a position as well. We stand on the path of restoration that we must take. Our families, our nations, and our world are all in this destiny. Therefore, even if we create a united world, the ultimate problem remains. How wonderful would it be if I could enter that united world and live happily? Now that the kingdom of heaven has come to this earth, how great would it be if we could live in that heavenly realm? But that is not possible. There are conditions that must be resolved. These conditions remain both externally and internally. Externally, there are the world, the nation, the people, and all of creation. Internally, there are our parents, spouses, and siblings centered on ourselves. We must resolve these issues. Without doing so, we cannot return.

When Jesus spoke to his mother, saying, "Woman, what do I have to do with you?" (John 2:4), this was not a casual remark. It was a serious statement that determined his life and death. He loved his parents, but he was in a position where he could not simply love them as they were. There was a need for resolution. Wouldn’t it be wonderful if we could just hold onto our siblings and love them? But that is not possible. We must return to our original position and love from there. To return, we must deny ourselves.

When Jesus saw his mother weeping while he was on the cross, he pointed to John and said, "Woman, behold your son" (John 19:26). Saying such a thing to a mother who was weeping for him is something that would not happen in this world. John was his son, and he was not her son. Jesus knew that he could not return to his mother, which is why he spoke that way.

After the resurrection of Jesus, when Mary Magdalene saw him and tried to hold onto him, he told her not to do so. Why? Because she had not yet reached a position where they could meet after resolving their issues. Therefore, even though Mary said, "Lord, I love you," she needed to go through a process of self-denial to return to a position where she could be positively received again. It is natural that Jesus would say such things to Mary, who had not yet reached a position of complete denial.

If I do not deny myself, I will be denied. 

From this perspective, when we consider the point of restoration, it is necessary for us to unify our nation and the world. We are moving forward with the desire for that. To achieve this, we must unite centered on God. To unite, we cannot simply remain as we are in our current environment. Even if there is a unified nation centered on God, I cannot simply become one with that nation. This principle still holds true.

Therefore, I must separate myself from the world of Satan. I must part ways with my nation that is in the realm of Satan. I must deny everything that I hold dear, all the material possessions I cherish, and any authority or glory I have pursued on this earth. To avoid being denied, I must first deny. If I deny first, I will not be tested by Satan. I will not be attacked by the enemy. If the enemy attacks me, the enemy itself will be destroyed.

In this light, we see that a person is a very simple existence, but in the historical process, they are a pivotal point. You must exist for your family to exist, for your nation to exist, for the world to exist, and for the universe to exist. If you do not exist, everything else is unnecessary. The restoration of the world is important, but the most pressing issue is oneself.

So, when we look at ourselves as individuals, what do I love? What do I like? What do I desire? Is it external or internal? Even in the world, do we not desire the internal? Is not our family, our internal family? Therefore, when the internal family is in a position of suffering, we will abandon everything external, no matter how precious, to protect that internal family. Isn’t this the normal state we recognize in today’s fallen world?

Then, can we just hold onto what is precious and return? The fall occurred through bloodlines and was caused by Satan’s false love. That is why we cannot simply return as we are. If that were possible, it would not have taken 6,000 years. If it were possible, Jacob would not have had to go through a path of suffering. Noah would not have had to endure 120 years of suffering. Jesus would not have needed to die. The family of Joseph would have sufficed. His brothers would have sufficed. The church would not be necessary.

For a new nation to be established, a new family must exist. If that could just happen as it is, if families could remain as they are, tribes could remain as they are, nations and the world could remain as they are, how wonderful would that be? That is what everyone desires. If that were the case, there would be no need for anything extraordinary. However, on the path of restoration, it does not work that way.

To receive God’s protection, 

I am not doing this because I am inferior to anyone else. I do not want to be insulted. I do not want to do this. It is simply that the path is such that I cannot avoid it. This position is a miserable one. I have a nation, but I cannot love it. If we look at our national anthem, it speaks of the East Sea and Baekdu Mountain enduring until the end, asking for God’s protection. But can God protect us? He cannot. When we confront a greater enemy and fulfill our duty before God, we can receive His protection, but if we fail to do so, we cannot receive it.

If the Republic of Korea is confronted by a greater nation, in other words, if it becomes weak against a greater enemy, then God will side with us. Why? Because the side that is being attacked is given priority in restoration. Abel was protected by God because he stood on the side of goodness, unlike Cain. However, when we cannot stand in such a position, we are the ones being attacked. When the Republic of Korea stands in a position of being attacked by the enemy, it is attacked from heaven.

So, when the Republic of Korea is in a position to be attacked by the enemy, who must be attacked? I must be attacked. The people of the Republic of Korea must be attacked. The people must suffer for the nation. The nation must suffer for the people. Without this, we cannot receive protection or sympathy from God.

In this light, within the nation, the family must stand in a position of unity, and within the family, the individual must stand in a position of unity. In other words, at the national level, the people must unite; at the ethnic level, the tribes must unite; at the family level, the families must unite; and at the individual level, the individuals must unite. This is because God protects those who stand in a position facing a greater enemy.

From this perspective, when we look at Jesus, he appeared alone with a global mission. Jesus thought that the world was with him, that the nation of Israel was with him, and that the people, tribes, and families of Israel were all with him. This is not a mere concept; it is a factual reality. When the family opposes Jesus, it becomes an enemy; when the tribe opposes him, it becomes an enemy; when the nation opposes him, it becomes an enemy; when the world opposes him, it becomes an enemy. The greater enemy is the problem.

Therefore, if we go out with the ability to fight against such an enemy, even if we die in battle, God will be on our side until that nation is destroyed. If we fought against the whole world, God would be on our side until the world is destroyed. Jesus fought centered on the world, transcending nations, so God supported him until that world was subdued. That is why Christianity has become a truly global religion.

Today, the Unification Church is in such a position. Those who lament this position are the ones who block the path to the world. Those who seek to escape this position are those who avoid the direct path to the world. You must understand this.

Even if we have all the necessary conditions today, they are merely means for tomorrow. They are not for today, but for tomorrow. Preparation is needed for a greater war. That is why it exists for tomorrow. Those who think it is for today will not be able to transcend to a higher world. In other words, they will not be able to establish a position. God says not to establish a position until He establishes it.

The people of Israel thought that God would send the Messiah based on the standard of having established a position, but they did not realize that he was sent to establish a position. That is why they lost even the nation of Israel. We must understand this today.

We have entered a path of destiny where we cannot simply go as we are with the external world. God is the Absolute Being, and that Absolute Being is our Father, and that Father is the Sovereign of heaven and earth. When we look at this again, that Absolute Being is the Father centered on me, the Sovereign centered on the world, and the center of heaven. That is why the term "Father" is precious. It is the closest title that can unify the spirit world, and it is also the closest title that can unify the world. We must have this conviction. We must have such a self-awareness. To have conviction, we must have faith. To have self-awareness, we must qualify to replace God. To govern creation in place of God, we must have a heart of love. It is impossible to govern without love.

The issue is how we realize this. Until we clearly understand how absolute that value is, we cannot resolve our issues.

We must have this realization. In other words, we must stand in a position higher than Adam and Eve before the fall.

What the Unification Church Must Do Today
So what is the most pressing issue for the members of the Unification Church today? It is self-awareness. 
You were born as new sons and daughters centered on God! This son and daughter cannot be exchanged for the whole world. Therefore, you cannot go back and forth! Just as winter passes and spring comes, just as the seasons change, my heart cannot change! Even if the seasons change, I will not deviate from the principle. 
You must be able to say that. Even if the external appearances are different, the inner self must be steadfast in its operation. 
What is the reason for denying oneself? It is to deal with the target of Cain's possible attacks. This is the highest strategy in evangelism. In other words, it means to go ahead before they attack. It means to go ahead and be their model. It means to be better than them. If you are worse than them, restoration cannot happen. That is why all the people who have corrected history until now have fought to be better than the people of their time. You must understand that they are the true saints. 
From the current standpoint of entering the 1970s, what must the Unification Church do today? We are in a position to unify the North and South centered on the nation. Some say the 1970s is the era of unification. So how do we achieve unification? While taking an offensive stance toward the North, we must also have a heart that sheds tears and prays for them. In other words, we ourselves must have a new awareness centered on God. We must regard God as the sovereign of heaven above and as our Father below. We must stand in the position that we exist for Him and on behalf of that nation. When we stand in that position, it is the same position where Jesus stood. That is, it is the position of Abel. It is a position that stands on behalf of heaven and a position that stands on behalf of the earth. It is the position of Abel. Without that awareness, one cannot become Abel. If this purpose is fulfilled, everything can be overcome without problems.

To love the nation, you must love it from the heavenly side, along with a new awareness. And you must deny. You must stand in a position where you lose even your own self and external appearances so that God can love you. 
Pray, and when you first receive grace through prayer, you will find that you cannot even meet your own mother. You must have that feeling. The fact that you have that feeling means you have become that close to God. Also, when you have a spiritual experience, even the husband or wife you have loved until now will appear like a snake. Just seeing them makes you feel uncomfortable. You must feel such things. Feeling that way is not bad. Behind that is the understanding that you are getting closer to God. Also, in the past, if your sons and daughters were hungry, you would bring them food and be so happy that you could die, but now you feel like you don’t want to see them. 
You feel like saying, “You brat, feel hungry.” You must have that kind of heart. Without feeling such things, you cannot meet the day of liberation. That is why it is said that when you enter the Unification Church, families are destroyed. Because such women come in... 
Restoration of Love
The fall is due to disbelief. Because of disbelief, we lost the essence and true love. So how many types of love are there? There is parental love, spousal love, and children's love; these three loves must be restored. This must be restored all at once. Then, if you enter into the realm where you can deny all these inner problems, what happens is 
you will feel that you are the son or daughter of God. You must feel that. You must feel it completely. You must feel that you are receiving God's love as a son or daughter. After that period passes, the next is the relative relationship. You will feel the love of a parent, and then the love of a spouse. 
So what mission should Christianity fulfill? It must fulfill the mission of being sons and daughters, then the mission of being bride and groom, and then the mission of being a father. Jesus fulfilled His mission during His 30 years of life, but His relationship with God was that of a parent and child. 
Jesus' 30 years of life was a life of fulfilling the mission of a son. After that, the history of Christianity until now is a history of seeking spousal love. When spousal love is found, parental love is established, and after that love is established, one can love children on behalf of God. If you look at it centered on yourself, it goes up in reverse: children's love, spousal love, parental love. You cannot restore without feeling such love centered on God. You must feel these three loves. 
Now, when we look at the members of the Unification Church centered on the Principle, it is unfortunate for the men, but what are men? The archangel's wife would originally become Adam's wife.

The desire to approach such a subject is the standard of the universal desire that exists today. 

The issue of love and the fulfillment of desires 
So, what is the center of uniting the world? It must be the realm of love. The Bible states that God is love, but the concept of love mentioned here is vague. The realm of love must be a value that can be higher than both the subject and the object. Only by entering such a position can unity be achieved. 

For humans, it is not only the reality that matters. Our desire is to extend our own life eternally, which is why people seek eternal life. Therefore, how to pursue eternal life beyond the limits of this life has been a concern for religious circles and good people seeking the world of conscience. When we consider our desires centered around these issues, it is possible to deduce that humans have a tendency to want to dominate not only the present but also the past. 

From this, it is clear that we humans are undoubtedly seeking an unchangeable absolute subjectivity in the past, present, and future. 

Our desires are not limited to that. Furthermore, we want to possess the created world, all things. We humans desire to own everything. When we see this, we realize that our desires have no boundaries. 

Thus, we can only conclude that there cannot be happiness without boundaries in desires. If there are no limits to desires, there cannot be a point of happiness. In a position where desires lead oneself, there can be no joy. Joy is something that can be felt when desires are fulfilled and one reaches a state of satisfaction. 

So, what allows this to happen? It is love. However, that love cannot conceive of eternal ideals if it cannot digest the boundaries of desire. From this perspective, we conclude that human desires must have boundaries. 

Then, what should set those boundaries? It must be something greater than what our own self demands or what the other demands. It must be in a position where the two can harmonize and mediate while possessing the perfect and eternal value of the present. What could that be? It must be the realm of love. 

So, when we look at ourselves today, what do we desire? We desire true love. Next, what do we desire? We desire true ownership. Then what do we desire next? We desire to establish a true relationship with God. Today, we are not causal beings but merely result-oriented beings. Therefore, we want to establish a relationship with the causal being. Until now, philosophy and religion have sought and pursued such things. 

We desire true people. We desire true things. We desire the true source. So, how can we possess true people, true things, and the true source, or the absolute? If I do not have the certainty to establish a relationship with them, I am unhappy. 

Then, what allows us to confidently stand in that position? It is nothing but love. That love is not love that originates from me. It is love that comes from the fundamental being. For the subject and I to unite in a relative position, there must be something that can respect the subject more than the object and the object more than the subject, something that has a value beyond the combined worth of the two. What could that be? It is the realm of love. It is the love realm that both consider important. 

When viewed from the perspective of the individual, it can be called love. 

Therefore, we must think about how to connect to that origin and seek the method. Without that, we cannot reach the realm of universal love. 

So, where should we start? Where should we begin? We must start from ourselves. We must go through the process of determining ourselves from a position that is not the subject. This is the standard of completion through the process of growth. In other words, we must start from ourselves. 

How should we love ourselves? 

That is why people love someone, right? They love themselves. However, until now, that love has been vague. So why do we love ourselves? Because the starting point to reach the absolute realm of love is oneself. We cannot reach the realm of universal love without connecting from ourselves. Therefore, we must have the content of love that can be absolute centered around ourselves. That is why we must love ourselves. 

The question is, how do we love ourselves? Is loving oneself a bad thing? No, it is good to love oneself. However, the issue is how to love. Today, we are trying to deny all relative relationships and establish ourselves from an independent position to love ourselves. Such love becomes a motive for failure the more we try. It brings about the breakdown of families horizontally and becomes a motive for the collapse of all history on a tribal level. 

So how should we love? We must love according to principles. In loving oneself, one cannot be the absolute subject. One is a result-oriented being. Therefore, one must not be a subjective being but must become an absolute object before the subject. Thus, until one reaches the boundary that a relative being must go, even if one loves oneself, one should not standardize oneself but should standardize the subject. Only then can I have the value to love myself as an object before the subject. This is something we have not known until now. 

You say you love your body, that you love yourself, but when is it possible to materialize that self-love? It is possible when you stand as a relative being before the essence that demands love centered around the ideal world. However, if you love yourself without standing in such a position, everything will fall apart. The entirety of your actions will not bear fruit in a way that can establish a relationship with the subject but will lead to destructive content. In this view, such societies or nations will perish.

Therefore, when you say you love yourself, you must clearly understand that this is not a subjective position. 

Loving oneself from the current position is meant to establish a perfect relative self before the eternal and unchanging subject. Therefore, when you stand in the position of having loved such a self, you will achieve unexpected results.

**Pioneer**

When we look at the historical process, when the flow of history moves in a bleak direction, those who stand in the position of creating that history become the guides of that era both temporally and historically. However, to become such a guide, one must inevitably bear the responsibility of a pioneer. 

Pioneers must be stronger than anyone else in pursuing a certain goal. This is because the struggle to find a new world entails risking faith and even life amidst hardships. Therefore, we must understand that the more difficult the path of the pioneer, the more the risks will increase proportionately. 

Thus, a pioneer must become a responsible figure who overcomes the unknown difficulties toward the destination. Without becoming a victor who has overcome such difficult processes, one cannot fulfill the justification of a pioneer. Therefore, wanting to be a pioneer is akin to a student needing a guide like a teacher. 

Even at this point when a nation is seeking a new path, a leader who plays the guiding role is necessary. Moreover, if we look at all the historical endeavors throughout history, it is the same. To pursue a new historical purpose and achieve that purpose, one must inevitably stand in the position of a pioneer bearing a difficult mission. We can see from the environmental conditions that without standing in the position of a pioneer, one cannot fulfill the role of a guide. 

From this perspective, in the providential course of restoring humanity, a guide centered on God's will is also necessary. Looking at the long history of 6,000 years, the will has developed from the individual to the family, lineage, nation, and the global providential era. 

To advance from the individual providential era to the family providential era, one must overcome and surpass the individual providential era. Here, as we rise from the family providential era to the national, state, and global providential eras, the need for pioneers and guides will increase proportionately. 

In the family of Adam, Abel could only fulfill the role of a guide after having completed the mission of a pioneer in restoring that era's family. To fulfill the mission of a pioneer, one must stand in an abnormal position rather than a normal one, and rather than being pushed back by unfavorable circumstances, one must overcome those circumstances and take a leading position to find a new path. In other words, one cannot fulfill the mission of a pioneer without standing in the position of aligning with the direction that can accomplish the purpose. 

The Path of the Pioneer 

From this perspective, when the mission of the pioneer is accomplished, one can finally take on the role of a guide. And the person who guides must set the direction for the followers. If that direction deviates or the purpose is misguided, the guide must play the role of correcting it in the middle. If followers deny this and try to go their own way, they will not even be able to properly determine their destination. 

A pioneer must be able to overcome all difficult conditions that arise in the process of pursuing a new purpose from a subjective position and in a multifaceted manner. Otherwise, one cannot be considered a pioneer. 

Therefore, only after fulfilling the mission of the pioneer can one walk the path of the guide and become a proper guide. 

Looking at the course of Noah, Noah also took on the role of a guide in heaven only after going through the mission of a pioneer representing the era in which he lived. Abraham also could only take on the role of a heavenly guide for individuals and societies after going through the mission of a pioneer. The same goes for Moses. Without going through the process of a pioneer, one cannot take on the responsibility of a guide. To move toward a new destination, one must explore it oneself. One must experience the pioneering content in reality. We know this well through history.

Without that, one cannot take on the historical, global, and cosmic role of a guide.

Only then is the true life of a leader determined. Being a leader is not something that is decided in an instant. When one stands in the position of resolving historical circumstances with the overall content centered on humanity, only then can one be recognized as a suitable leader before God.
