Live a stimulating life
The same goes for the lives of ordinary ministers. When they give lectures in their region or district, the members think, "Oh! The regional leader is giving a principle lecture. After that, this phrase will come out," and they all know it. Therefore, one cannot just give the same lecture now as they did three years ago. In the past, lectures were given in that way, but now one must add branches to it and know how to lecture with new explanations and content. In terms of content, one must share experiences necessary for spiritual development. One must give lectures that fit the atmosphere of the time.

If you have been in ministry for three years, you must at least share a story that can provide stimulation to the members. Members who do not feel this sense of reality do not attend Sunday worship well. From this perspective, you can see that you have been too negligent in your lectures until now. Therefore, starting from now, you must present something new. You must give stimulation by any means necessary. You must supplement it through prayer. If that does not work, you must negotiate with your life on the line.

Even when you walk, you must have a mindset of seeking something new. Also, do not just go to church. When you go to church, you must go with the mindset of encountering new positions and environments to create something new. It is not just about going in a straight line to church; sometimes you must take a detour. You should go south, but also try going north. This is to find a new path.

If you still do not feel that sense of reality, try changing all the household items. Do not just leave them as they are for months. Turn everything upside down. Then your thoughts will change. This is absolutely necessary.

Even when praying, the feeling is different when praying in front versus praying in the back. The feeling is also different when praying among the audience. Therefore, how to create environmental changes is necessary. If you experience mystical prayers, they are fundamentally different from ordinary prayers. The east and west, south and north, and center are all different.

To experience new feelings, you must change your living environment. In other words, to change your heart in your life, it is essential to remodel your environmental conditions. If a husband works in a company, it is not fun to always deal with him in the same meaningless way every time he commutes.

A play, simply put, is about laughing and crying. A play is about making people laugh and cry, so why do people like it and pay to go see it? Because when they watch it, they laugh from different angles. Similarly, crying is also done from different angles. It is necessary to see things from different perspectives. Why do people pay to go see it? Because they can feel something new from a different angle and receive stimulation that can impact new fields and gain income.

When you stand on the podium to lead the public, you must do everything. When praying, you must pray poetically and intellectually. You must expand your new emotional content while encountering various circumstances. This is absolutely necessary for a minister's life.

When this lifestyle becomes habitual, you can talk about one topic in various directions. You can discuss it from many aspects. When you look from the east to the west, the scenery looks different. Even if a fight breaks out while passing through the neighborhood, it may seem unrelated to you, but it is not coincidental. Through that, you must reflect on whether you have a talent for fighting in the streets.

You may think it has nothing to do with you, but can you definitively say that such people will not appear in your children or grandchildren? You cannot be sure. It is certainly not someone else’s problem. Such things can happen at any time.

Therefore, as you live each day, you must build good relationships with the given environment and realize something new from there, and you must connect that realization with God. How you plant that connection in front of many people is the responsibility of a minister.

Thus, do not lose what you have experienced. You must test it with someone. You must give it to them. Then you will know what the result will be. This is how something new is obtained. Ultimately, it is not about becoming a large vessel all at once. It is through long periods of lonely, hard experiences that one learns to understand others.

Therefore, you must first determine your position to appear as a new subjective entity in understanding others.

Now, as you finish your training and return, some may have a more complicated heart than when they came. Some may struggle to solve the difficult situations of the regional headquarters, while others may be worried about their personal issues; there will be all kinds of people. So how will you solve those problems?

You must not say, "Oh, I’m going to die." You must return with a new heart, a new standard, a new resolution, and a new direction.

Until now, I had to cry in a difficult position, but now I must handle my new self that must make a new start from a new angle, and I must act with a new resolution centered on God. To find solutions, you must be determined to take any risks. If you do not, you must understand that you will retreat on your path. During this training period, you may gain a lot, but what you gain may also have a counterproductive effect that could break you.

Now we bear the heavenly mission to develop ourselves anew as we face the 1970s. This is the inevitable task that the current era demands of us. Therefore, you must fundamentally change this spiritual life and create new factors of inspiration within your daily life. Only by expanding the foundation of life through practical experiences can new development occur. Even though the place you must go is still far away, you must not continue in the same way as now.

Thus, if you have listened to a story for one hour, you must tell it for three hours. You must speak until your voice is hoarse. As someone responsible, you must deliver the word; if you cannot speak because your voice is hoarse, what should you do? You must be able to convey emotion even by mimicking gestures, eye movements, and foot movements. You must go out with that resolve.

You cannot think that after eating three meals a day normally, you will cultivate life in your spare time. You must cut away what is wrong. Cultivating one life is not an easy task. It requires sincerity. You cannot do it with leftover things. You cannot do it with scraps left over from meals. You must decisively cut those things away. God is with those who are in such positions.

The essential attitude a minister must have
You must develop your lifestyle in this way. The first thing must be offered to God. The first fruits must be dedicated to God. Where there are no first fruits, God does not accompany you. Where there is no newness, God does not accompany you. You must understand this. Offerings cannot be made from what others have left behind. That is tainted. Those who have received grace can recognize this immediately. That is why they are kept from unclean places.

Therefore, you must directly experience a life that can stimulate something new, focusing solely on God. When you feel that heart while working, there will surely be multiplication. Then, there will be development. Living trees produce new buds. Yesterday and today are different.
There is definitely a vitality there. On the other hand, a tree without roots is a dead tree. It means that things change differently from yesterday to today. The day you lose such feelings, you should pray as if your life depends on it. You must accumulate sincerity, even if it means staying up all night to pray. God may intentionally take away that time from you if you try to live such a life. If that happens, no matter how hard you try, you will not be able to find hope. There are times when the more you try, the deeper you fall into a dark predicament. At such times, you must have the determination to serve God by even making the accompanying Satan submit to your side and fight even stronger.

If you say one wrong word, the impact can last for days or even weeks. If you feel a pang of conscience, it can last for months. You may not have experienced such feelings, but you must realize how much heaven cares about you during those times. So how important is a single word? You need to understand how to approach the fundamental attitude when dealing with the life issues of others. You must deeply feel the urgency of such matters.

For the nation, mere patriotism is not enough. You must become a patriot. Only by acting as a patriot with a sense of patriotism can you bear fruit. That is the decisive factor on the realistic stage. You have followed the path of purpose for several years until now. However, if you have spent your time muddling through with the standards of today, that time will pass without any reward.

I must delve into the very foundation of life and observe all realities. From that position, I must bring forth something new. Have you ever held such a heart? During the 24 hours of a day, how much have you worked with purpose at the center, and how much have you felt the value of that purpose as you moved forward? You must consider how many hours that actually amounts to. We need times when we can do that.

Additionally, you must have times when you can confirm what you believe through your sensory organs, that is, through intuition. How much time you have for such experiences is important. Those who focus on their personal lives may not feel it well, but those who live a life of grace feel that everything they see is different from the past. It is always new. It feels new in the morning and new in the evening. When God's grace gradually rises, one feels the mystery in three dimensions. If there is someone who can sense that, they are a happy person. Such a person stands in a position where they can praise their nobility while feeling the infinite value that Buddha spoke of when he said, "In heaven and on earth, I alone exist."

As you follow the purpose and live your faith, when you reflect on your past, you will feel that the past is pulling you. Therefore, you wish to return to that good past. Some long-time members may say that the 1960s were good. You must know how to take the essential attitude you need to have. You must ponder such issues. It cannot be as it is now. You must stand in a position where you can feel something new even through your senses to achieve significant development.

Become a foundation that can stimulate God.
Now, as you finish your training and return to your respective places, you will face your wives or children. Then ask your child, "What kind of father do you want me to be?" How do you think they will answer? This is a significant issue. Do they want you to be a father whom God loves? Do they want you to be a father who is loved by the people of South Korea? Or do they want you to be a father who can be liked by your children or mother? They may initially want you to appear as a father who can be liked in their eyes, but their inner desire is for you to be a father who can be liked by the world. Isn't that your family? They will also want you to be a father who can be liked by God. Thus, they will wish for you to be a father who can leave behind all the blessings of the heavenly world for future generations. When you think of this, the issue becomes serious.

And when I say my children are beautiful, what standard do I base that on? Did I say they are beautiful from the perspective of a physical parent with physiological emotions? Or did I say they are beautiful as a son of God who can connect to the heavenly realm? The issue is significant.

The same goes for how you treat your wife. You should not approach her with the mindset that you are my wife and I am your husband, so you must live this way. There are ties of heaven and earth intertwined in that relationship. You must innovate the habitual attitudes that countless couples have had until now. So, you must do well.

Whether you are dealing with God or your descendants, you must become a foundation that can eternally stimulate God and be a motive that can add to Him. You must become a couple with such content. In conclusion, when a husband treats his wife or a wife treats her husband, they must think of their relationship as one that cannot be seen even among the greatest masterpieces, and they must live swearing to each other before heaven and earth. There is a need to study and seek when that time will be. When viewed from that perspective, there is no limit for a heartfelt couple, as they can develop infinitely centered on the spiritual world, and there is content that can stimulate others.

So, you must excavate that. It is necessary.

Why is adolescence such a good time in life? It is a time that will not be forgotten throughout one’s life. At that time, it feels like you can control the world with your hands. It seems like the world can be grasped in your hands. Everything you encounter feels new. In spring, seeing the snow piled in the valley melt and cause a landslide makes you marvel greatly. It looks magnificent. You also find it wonderful to see a fawn that is startled and runs away. Everything feels free, stimulated by infinite value, and possesses the capacity to absorb and relate to oneself; that is precisely the time of adolescence.

The period of adolescence is when the passion of love and the new world are keenly felt, and it is a time when growth occurs in all directions. It is like the spring when barley grows lushly.

However, among those lush leaves, only one stalk must emerge. But where that stalk will come from is uncertain. The same goes for the position of adolescence. Those leaves can spread out in all directions, replacing the stalk, and it is a time that stimulates the existence that can hold an infinite creative world.

The same applies to faith life. No matter how old you are, there should be a feeling that is sensed in some way. When you call your grandmother, it should not just end with calling her; you must meet her with feelings beyond just calling her. It is through such feelings that you can become closer than anyone else in the emotional realm. 

Having such feelings will allow you to surpass the entrenched emotional foundation of the satanic world and evoke a new spring's stimulation.

In other words, you must prepare the capacity to emerge as a subjective being that can recreate the conditions of adolescence and win. It is not about boasting about the Unification Church or discussing how things are. Just because you have had new experiences with God does not mean that reproduction will occur immediately. You must establish a foundation where you can unite with God from a new position along with new experiences, and from that foundation, the capacity to adapt and reproduce anew will arise.

Be a Unificationist who embodies the principles.
You must adapt to these principles. Then your attitude toward life will change from what it has been until now. Think about our Unification Church. Everything is good. The principles are good. Then how well do we know God? Setting aside the existence of the spiritual world, if someone thinks the Unification Church is nothing special, that person is crazy.

This can be understood through the testimonies of many people in this era. If the Unification Church has the principles that make known the reality of God, what more could we ask for!

However, people say that the Unification Church has good principles and everything, but they lack money. Well, what will you do with money? Can you exchange God for money? Can you exchange the principles for money? We possess infinite value that cannot be exchanged for anything. Can you weigh this on a scale? Even if you placed the whole world on it, it cannot be weighed, yet those who think it is cheap are crazy. They are thoroughly insane.

When you think about it, how many people among the world's population believe that there is a spiritual world? How many pastors know that fact? They do not know. However, even if you appear externally to have nothing and look shabby, you undoubtedly know these facts, so you are in a position to assert confidently 100% on the path we are taking. Therefore, you should realize that you are better than those pastors.

When you consider this value, you could speak from a place that shines brighter than diamonds, yet there are people who seek to go to a place like a dung heap. So, you must completely die to yourself. You must strive to develop anew according to the principles and bloom brightly. You must make it possible to manifest under the conditions presented by the principles. The spiritual world must also be able to appear brightly. This is the issue you should be thinking about; what does money matter? Money will simply follow.

To reach such a realm, you must enter another person's house with a husband and insist on taking that lady away for more than a year. I do not mean to take her away in a bad sense. If you can touch her heart and impress her in every way, she will surely follow you. Unificationists must have the confidence that they can do anything.

Without doing so, you cannot control the great battles ahead. It means you cannot subdue the satanic world. Therefore, you must experience everything. To do so, you must set aside your pride and, regardless of what the husband says, sit down and convey the words. When that happens, you will not be able to speak carelessly. Only then will authority arise. When you go out centered on such tremendous authority and power, they will welcome you.

You are a man who can melt the world, yet what is this! You are not even as good as a pawn in a game; how trivial is that? You must not remain in such a lazy position.

Just as I have laid a spiritual foundation through global activities until now, you must also engage in such activities. If you have such a tremendous background but cannot act, that is trivial. Just by being born as a child of the True Parents, you can hum a that it is good. That is your original feeling.

Even if you eat bad food that even a beggar would not eat, you must defend your position. The time will come soon. You must overcome until then.

The difference between those who prosper and those who fail.
From this perspective, what more do you expect here? In this operational era, you must wear silk clothes inside and rags outside. You must do so for operational reasons. Your fate is not such; it is for operational reasons that you must do this. Until now, we have centered on this. The fact that I have been shackled without any sin is also part of that operation. Do not think that I must escape from that environment and live.

Just wait and see! No matter how much you strike me, I will eventually acquire the absolute conditions that can completely subdue you. That is what must be done.

Even so, this is not about taking off the ragged clothes; it is about stripping off even the silk clothes inside and running around in just your bare skin. Who will sympathize with that? Such a person deserves to be scorned. You should be trampled upon wherever you go, chased away. You must receive forgiveness. That is what I think. I have suffered and starved because I am inadequate.

I have also been in hiding and experienced hunger. For a month or two, I went around begging for food. When I fled, I left last after everyone else had gone. That was because wherever I went, there was rice, and I wanted to take that rice with me. If you see that, it might seem like stealing since I am taking someone else's belongings, but when there is no owner on the way to flee, it becomes the property of the townspeople, so taking it all is not a crime. If you take it, they will be grateful instead.

When I begged for food, I went to the threshold of that house to receive it. The food received in that way digests better. The more you eat, the more delicious it is. You may have experienced this. When you have been starving for days and then get to eat one meal, you eat it in an instant, right? Even the ceremonial rice feels good to eat.

I remember that day was in late January. During the chaos, I did not need a blanket. To go to Busan, carrying a blanket would be a burden, so I sold everything and exchanged it for a sack of rice. At that time, there was no rice. Because there was no rice, I exchanged it for barley and sweated profusely while trampling it down. I said to the people who came down with me, "Let's eat well." At that time, we had no choice but to eat. Not having a blanket did not mean we would freeze to death.

That would be about half a bowl of soybeans. We made all of that into rice cakes and sat down to eat together. (Laughter) We even saved about one bowl to give to the hostess. Since we had not eaten much, we enjoyed eating like that.

Even in such circumstances, when it became really difficult, God helped me. He prepared food for me. Sometimes, an unfamiliar lady would come out of her house and greet me as a precious guest. When I asked why, she said that in her dream, she was told to welcome a precious guest. That means the spiritual world was already cooperating through that person. So, you will absolutely not starve to death. Such things happen to me quite often. Because of that, I do not worry about such matters even now.
Will I tremble? (laughs) I haven't experienced that. When I think about not repaying my debts and being attacked by creditors, I wonder what God, who is watching, would think about that, and it seems impressive. So, whatever happens, everything is part of one's destined fate. There's nothing to think differently about.

A person preparing for tomorrow
What you all say is difficult is just a pretense. It sounds like a pretense to me. Who set the standard that life is difficult until now? Who set the standard that you must eat three meals a day? Did God set it, or did you, who are clever, set it? Who set it? Following this standard feels unpleasant, and saying it's difficult makes no sense. From now on, one meal a day is the standard of living. What if that one meal is barley rice and soybean paste stew? What will you do if that is your fate and your standard of living? Think of it as the standard of living you absolutely hoped for. Shouldn't it be that way?

In the old days, people living by foraging fruits would consider eating barley rice a great honor, right? Living in a community and being able to eat barley rice is a precious position. They would have regarded it as a great pride and thanked God for it. It means to return to that primitive position where you can thank God even while eating barley rice. If I farmed and grew barley rice for the first time, would I feel bad or good? How delicious would it be?

Who set your living standards? You have been habitually eating three meals a day until now. But because that has been well established, it becomes a problem. If there is nothing, you should know how to go hungry. If going hungry is my life, then so be it. If I happen to eat a full meal one day, then I can set that as my standard of living. What is there to worry about? Can we start anew with the idea of debt forgiveness and return, while doing everything and seeing everything like in the world?

The other day, this pastor was in a fuss over something. So I told him to stop right away. It's not that I don't know that pain. I've experienced all those things too. From that position, call out to God! Then the sound of that call changes. When you reach that position, you must become serious. Without seriousness, miracles do not happen.

New world inventions occur during the process of war. It happens in times of emergency for the whole world. Why? Because it is serious. In that sense, war has greatly contributed to creating wisdom in human history. This is serious.

Think about the moment you decide whether it’s my son or daughter, my nation, or my country? There must be such a time. Will I live or die? Will I go or not? I must carry all the hard work I've put in until now. But if an unsatisfactory result comes out, how do you push it away? Even if you find yourself in such an environment, you must overcome it. In all those environments, what will you set as your standard? If there is no standard, there will be nothing new. Is there anything to be thankful for? So, even while drinking a bowl of water, maintain a grateful heart.

When I receive a meal, I remember the life in prison where I had to scoop rice with my fingers. So, whenever I visit a family, I don’t like it when they prepare a lavish feast for me, saying that I came. I would rather have tattered clothes and eat barley rice, where everyone can sympathize and cannot help but shed tears. That is what I demand from people. What is there? There is tomorrow.

If you become complacent thinking everything is fine without a prepared standard, then tomorrow will be blocked, and hope will end. Therefore, a man who dreams of tomorrow with hope and prepares is more formidable than a person who is complacent about success. You must think this way. But what is there to worry about? You should suffer more than I have. These days, you eat barley rice, right? Try eating pure barley rice. If you have eaten this rice until now, you should also try eating barley rice.

I thought meeting my husband would be good, but there are times when it’s bad. You cannot only expect good things. Can you just bask in sunlight for 24 hours? There must be night, right? Isn’t it a principle that what is high becomes low?

The living standard of pioneers
Our Unification Church has been trampled by the world until now, but even so, it says to give to others even if I cannot eat in that position. By doing so, you can rise to a higher place, and thus you will not perish. Therefore, if you want to feel something new centered around your living standards, you must enter the lowest position.

The other day, when I came to church early, a sewage truck was there, using a hose to clean out the church's restroom. But it seems that a rag got stuck at the end of the hose. So I waited for about 15 minutes, and because of the smell and boredom, someone next to me was saying something, so I said, “Hey, just stay still. Do you know how good that smell is?” But if you think of it negatively, you cannot endure it. If you think of bad things positively, a new world opens up there.

Therefore, the question is how to become a subject that can digest everything. The problem is how to create a self that can digest whatever it eats. A person who has the ability to eat anything that comes their way and digest it survives. Therefore, you should not be picky about what you eat.

Now, let’s conclude. You must become a new human and start anew. Look at things in a new way. If you have seen a neighborhood, recognize that neighborhood anew. Think deeply with a sense of longing. When I see a big pond, I think, “When summer comes, I will take a good bath!” If there is a very high and wide place, I will roll around to my heart's content! Think differently from ordinary people.

Isn’t it spring now? Many of you will be going down south. When you go down there, you will see flocks of ducks and geese flying north as the season changes. There are also many fields there. You must be able to run freely in such places. There must be something like that. A pioneer must have such a mindset to pioneer.

But will you just sit still and watch if your family comes or not? When your family comes, you think, “Oh, will the rice bin be filled with rice or not?” You think like that, right? (laughs) It’s not that they like anything given to them like beggars. If they don’t give, will they just starve to death? Even wild boars can eat well on their own...

Do you know how nutritious the roots of arrowroot are? If you are really hungry, take a pickaxe and go up the mountain to dig up some arrowroot to eat. If you go and dig for about a week, you can eat enough for a month even if you can’t eat anything else. So what’s the fuss? What is there to worry about? If you go up the mountain, you can eat arrowroot and grass roots... So you just need to know how to dig them well. Even living on just that can be beneficial, right? Think that way. If you do, you will never die.

In summer, I can live without a handful of rice. If I have a needle and two yards of thread, I can live. I use that to fish. (laughs) Then why would I die? Why would I starve? I absolutely will not starve.

In autumn, wherever you go, there is plenty to eat. Even if you dig sweet potatoes, you can gather ears of grain from the field and eat as much as you want. Would God say, “You are not my son because you do such things, so I will take you out of the family tree”? There is no such God. God can bless and appreciate such things, so there are times when those things are necessary. I have also done such things. After doing such things, I feel good. When I dig sweet potatoes, I always leave a few roots behind. I have done all that in the past. Later, when I dig up the sweet potatoes I left behind, seeing the bright red sweet potatoes revealed makes me feel really good. That feeling is better than winning money at a gambling table. There is no comparison.

What’s wrong with doing a little bit of that? There is nothing wrong with it. There are various ways to live. But who set the principle that you must eat three meals a day? Who set it? Did God say to do that? Do not set such a standard.

Effort and achievement
I am not afraid even if I go into prison now. That is heaven. It starts anew from there. Even if they give me barley rice, that’s fine. Bring me rotten, smelly soybean paste soup. I will eat it while reciting a thousand-year history, thinking, “How delicious this is! What did my ancestors think while eating such rice?” I think this way, so my dimension is different. That moment is serious.

Even if I sleep next to a latrine, I think, “How fortunate! Isn’t this a good opportunity to shine my life and grasp the history of humanity?” That’s how I think. Don’t think negatively. I thought that way and came out. It’s the same now.

Not long ago, when I visited a factory, the production manager reported the situation inside, but it didn’t resonate with me. He thought it would take several months, but I instructed him to complete it by the 23rd. So if he couldn’t do it as promised, he would have to face serious consequences. But if I say something, it would be a matter of his pride... So I watched quietly for a few days. One evening, he came to me, saying he couldn’t work that evening. These guys met the wrong person. I said, “From now on, we are starting again, so everyone gather.” This is public, so I said if it’s not done by midnight, they can’t go home. Then they started working again. But if they worked like that, they wouldn’t finish even if it was past midnight. The time they started working was around 9 PM, and even if I left them alone until 10, 11, and midnight, they finished everything.

Because I ordered it, they had to finish it, even if it meant staying up all night. They got the hint. So they completed what could be done in a day in just three hours. They finished everything by midnight. See, there’s nothing that can’t be done.

That’s how I set my standards. If I eat like others, dress like others, and work on the same schedule as others, when will I ever get ahead of others? You must work hard day and night.

Just yesterday, I came home after midnight, went to bed around 12:30, and woke up around 2:15 AM. What do you think I did? I prayed. I prayed until 4 AM, and when I heard the siren, I knocked on Mother’s room. If I knock before that, it would be rude. I went into the room around 4:15 and hurried to get ready to go to the factory, arriving there by 5:30.

I waited for about three hours until they came to work. How do you think that waiting felt? It was truly enjoyable. Waking up early while everyone else is asleep and having a new mindset feels good.

If I worked like this yesterday, I would tell myself that if I can’t work like this today, it’s a motivation. Then the employees get excited and work. That makes me feel very good. Even fatigue depends on the situation. If the mood is good, fatigue runs away.

You should try it once. There are times when I feel sleepy if I just sit still. But I cannot allow myself to comfortably doze off while young people are working. I cannot do that. I absolutely cannot. However, when I am too tired, I sometimes ask God for forgiveness and take a short nap, but I do not sleep at my own convenience. No matter how tired I am, I do not just collapse on the spot. I will collapse only after I have achieved my desired goal, not before.

I still live with that standard. Therefore, experiences or lifestyles in good places are not absolute. Discover something new... You must discover something new. Older people may be tired, but if they stand in opposition to conventional things, God will be with them. God will surely be with them.

What should older people do to walk the path of purpose? If the body weakens, there will be many restrictions in physiological functions. How should we reinforce this? I am researching this. In an era where spirit and body must act together, what will happen if we keep weakening? I am currently preparing for that. How about I teach you that?

So what is the problem? We must make a new start. To make a new start, you must discover something new every day. A person who discovers something new will never be left behind. Even if they face difficulties, they will never be discouraged. Instead, it becomes fun.

Earlier, Han In-soo came to visit and said that sitting in the office at the Victory Federation is dull, but seeing the district leaders reminds him of the time when he was responsible for the church and worked with his life on the line. He said he missed that time with the members he had come to see. I understood well. He has finally matured.

In the spirit world, that is the only thing to boast about. In the spirit world, having a lot of money is not something to brag about. You cannot boast about having power in the world either. What matters is how many lives you have saved. Whether you are a noble or a commoner, or whether you transcend tribes, how many nations have you related to new life and saved? That is the true wealth. That is the only wealth.

In the spirit world, there is nothing that is lacking, so there is nothing to miss, but if there is something to miss, it is a true person. Therefore, those who have devoted effort to nurture true people will naturally become glorious sons and daughters in the heavenly world. So, that is the only thing you can boast about. 

Among you, there may be someone who has lived as a district leader for more than ten years, but that is not important. Whether it’s ten years or several decades, it doesn’t matter.
Even if I say so, it is the same. The other day, I heard reports that a few people received the handover up to the 17th phase as regional leaders, but if they received the 108th phase instead of the 17th, what does it matter? More than that, we need to take people as the center and observe them. Those who have not experienced this cannot do it. They lack qualification. Centered on God's love, we must meet people, stay up all night discussing the future, recite poetry while looking at the sun, or feel something while gazing at the flowing river. Without experiencing emotions that one has never felt in any literary work through the connections between people, one cannot become a child of God. Living while feeling that is what makes life enjoyable as a human being.

Longing for people
When discussing life issues with connected individuals, plan to completely conquer that person within three hours while observing their expressions. The thrill of tightening the conversation over 10 minutes, 20 minutes, or an hour is greater than the feeling of drawing the last card after betting everything you have at a gambling table. While gambling ends once it's done, relationships with people do not end there. They continue to develop. Branches keep extending from there. If nurtured well, they spread in all directions. Have you ever felt something more valuable than this?

From this perspective, the most precious and important position in the Unification Church is that of a district leader. When you become a district leader, you oversee about one-third of the province, so there is enough work to be done on a stage that size. In South Korea, to run for a National Assembly seat, one focuses on one district, but as a district leader, you can command and move across three districts. Is being a National Assembly member a problem? It is something you can do. It means you can achieve anything. Additionally, it is a good environment where you can be hired in various fields at the center.

With such a stage before you, can you say you cannot work because you lack money? As long as your body is alive, is a flaw really a problem? The issue is aging, not lacking money.

Why is that? If you do not genuinely long for people, they will absolutely not long for you. Therefore, ministers must always wake up early, keep the door open, and wait for people until after four o'clock, listening for the first crow of a rooster. If the rooster crows first, you should think, "Ah, that rooster is up before me." You should even complain about it. If you do not do this, your members will not wake up in the early morning, will not long for you as their teacher or leader, and will not pray. Where can results appear without motivation?

Today, that is how it is for you in the Unification Church. Unification Church members scattered around the world only cling to you, saying, "Teacher, teacher! There are these issues, please help us," but they do not think about these things. If they do not think about these things, they will be punished. You owe a debt to the teacher in this regard. Since you owe a debt, you must repay it. You should at least bring your food to those children. Since you are in a position to give, it would be an honor for you to give it joyfully. That is how the teacher thinks.

A tower built with effort does not collapse. The problem lies here. 

How much have you longed for this person? Even if I explain it, you will not understand. How much have you longed for God's sons and daughters? How much have you longed for the hopeful family, the hopeful nation, the hopeful country, and the hopeful world? You do not know that. For that, money is not the issue. Even if you act like a beggar, longing for people is glorious. Forgetting the glory of the world and trying to pave the way for heaven is glorious. That is a wonderful thing.

Methods for developing spiritual sensitivity
If you have a longing for someone, even if there is a wall preventing you from meeting that person, something will happen that transcends that wall. Even if I keep my mouth shut, such things will happen. The spirit world will fill that gap. Even when I was in the Hungnam prison, I did not preach with words. I preached without words. The spirit world mobilized to cooperate. If they did not, it would have been a big problem.

It is the same. Therefore, even when you go to the local areas, you must do the same. How is the local area? In the 1960s, I visited all the famous places. I regret not being able to walk barefoot across the beautiful land of Korea in the past. I have been to every village…. Now I cannot do that because I cannot do what I need to do.

I would like to be a county head, going to every household in the village and getting a bowl of water. Don't you wonder what kind of house there is in this village, or what kind of people live in that village? If you do not do that, you cannot be a leader.

Today, think about what kind of person you will meet on your way. Consider what the first person you meet will be like, what the second person will be like, and what the third person will be like. Pray, "Father, what kind of person will I meet? I hope to meet such a person." If what you thought and prayed aligns perfectly, it feels good. By having such experiences, your spiritual sensitivity develops.

When you set out on the road, you will already have a feeling that you will meet a certain type of person today. The spirit of a person connects infinitely. If you think you will meet a certain person today and then actually encounter that person, you will be surprised, saying, "Oh my!" This happens often when your thoughts align with the inspiration taught by the spirit world. You must accumulate such experiences. Do you understand? "Yes."

Through such intuition and premonition, you can understand people's emotions and predict the fate of a nation. You must develop your spiritual sensitivity through these experiences. Then, you will also begin to think about how this country will be in the 1970s. You can think about that while walking, whether you are in an empty place or a solemn one.

The true meaning of hardship
In your faith life, even if there are some annoying things, it does not matter. If God were to walk this path, how would He walk it? People might think this way, but I can also think differently.

And if you have good experiences, you should have the desire to record at least a page about them in your journal. That record will remain in your history for a long time. It will be an invaluable record in your life of faith. Not being able to do that would be a regret.

You may have once taken a train without a ticket to come up to Seoul from the countryside. Sitting in the very back, you were anxious, wondering when the conductor would appear, right? When the conductor did show up, you would hide like a mouse, and only after the conductor passed would you finally breathe a sigh of relief. Yet, you would feel that those times were good. The feelings from that time are something you cannot experience in another world.

Following the Unification Church, such things have happened. In fact, it was wrong not to buy a ticket with money. Instead, you should give even more significant help for this country. Personally, you should give more than that. You may have to face legal consequences for your actions. However, when you work in a public capacity, you are not bound by any conditions in the heavenly realm. Therefore, while hardship was present, it was good at that time.

The teacher also has memorable experiences. When I was transported to Hungnam prison with handcuffs alongside robbers, I still vividly remember walking along the creek path as I entered the mountain valley. I cannot forget that time when I walked along the winding mountain paths. It was an impressive step toward a new world.

What will be the path I must take every day in the future? After finishing my sentence, what should I do? I am very curious about that. How do I navigate prison life? It is difficult, but I will go. That time became a good opportunity to awaken a new self. What remains for the teacher is nothing but that.

At one time, I worked digging tunnels in Hamhung. While working in extreme hunger, my hands holding the pickaxe could not lift, and my spirit was exhausted.

When I heard the call for lunchtime, I cannot express how delighted I was. That meal! The feeling of putting the pickaxe into the ground and turning around for that meal, the teacher has countless materials from such mountain histories. No hardship can compare to that.

These miserable stories should not destroy me; rather, they should shine brightly in history. Therefore, we must go until the day we can gather the treasures that God has kept. When we share such suffering with all humanity, just speaking about it for ten minutes will bring more tears than preaching for an hour on a different topic. Where else can you find such good sermon material?

Thus, I tell you not to worry and to endure hardships until you are 30 years old. Jesus also suffered until he was 33 before facing death. The blessings of the Unification Church that the teacher speaks of are blessings that you have borrowed. You must clearly understand that.

What is the conclusion of all this content? It is to realize something new. Only by realizing something new can a new day come. If something new does not emerge, there can be no development. Even though Mother is sitting here, it seems the teacher is discussing various topics, but because Mother listens most seriously, she ultimately understands what the discussion is about. The conclusion is that this conversation is about oneself. Therefore, extensive education is necessary. You must educate yourself a lot.

Contributors before the will
In practical life, the teacher lives a strict life. Those who have been close to me know well. You must cultivate yourself. You need to give yourself new stimuli. If you deny that, you will lead a dry and flavorless life. Then God will also become flavorless. Do you prefer a flavorless life? When watching a comedy or tragedy, dramatic scenes emerge, right? What are those dramatic scenes? They are based on three-dimensional content that can move people, which is why everyone is interested. Thus, good movies centered on love draw large crowds.

Similarly, you must become actors in the establishment of God's kingdom. Do you understand? You must be in a position to influence many people with heartfelt and moving content.

Preaching is the same. When you enter a lecture, you should observe the atmosphere and think about what to say to that person, how to lead this person, and then speak accordingly. When you experience this, you will know that God is with you. That is necessary. You must experience that God is alive; you must not feel that God is dead.

When you experience that God is alive, even if you are told not to evangelize, you will inevitably evangelize. Evangelism is the most shocking thing and creates something new. If there are ten people, having serious conversations with them will transform all ten into new individuals. Then, you should ask them to come to church and pray. When they develop, you will inevitably develop as well. You will rise.

If you step on grass, it will spring back, right? Similarly, when they jump, you will also jump. Isn't that right? Therefore, living for heaven has no negatives. Because God is with you, there are no negatives, as development occurs. If that person does not bear fruit, I will bear fruit.

Think about this position, and when each of you goes down to your church, you should have a different feeling than when you came up on the Gyeongbu line or the Honam line. If you came up seeing Seoul, you should also look at Seoul when you go down. There must be a standard. You need that.

When you get into the car, you should think about what kind of person you will meet today. When you find that person, observe them until you reach your destination. You may not know well, but think, "That person seems to have a hasty personality," or "That person seems to have a good personality." If I do this, that person will surely react this way. Test it out. If it matches what you thought, it will feel exhilarating.

Do the same in your neighborhood. "Oh! That lady must have this kind of personality. If I act this way, she will likely respond this way." Then, naturally go out and bump into her without letting her know. What will you do if you bump into her unknowingly? Will you hit her? At that time, you will be able to understand that person's personality. Then, apologize. Through such experiences, you will gather data.

Now, let us conclude. Let us all start anew. To do that, the question is how much newness you possess. God does not take anything that is not the first, that is, something new. You must firmly understand this and eliminate the concepts you have had until now in relation to the principle teachings, family life, or evangelism. You must stand in the position of replacing the heart of the Creator who creates new things in a new field and resolve to become a contributor in seeking new standards that elevate infinite value. If you become such a person, you will never fail. He will always develop because heaven is with him. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Words> In our Unification Church, the term blessing is generally directly associated with marriage. 

Among the countless people living on this earth, there are many who wish to be happy. Many hope to inherit some legacy from their ancestors, and many wish to inherit wealth from their parents. However, in order to inherit from parents, one must be the child who is most beloved among siblings, so that the parents can say, "I will give you all that I have." In other words, one cannot receive an inheritance without going through a period of being recognized by the parents, nor can one enter the position of receiving a blessing. 

The origin and conditions for the blessing
When we consider the term blessing centered on the will today, we understand that this term did not begin with the Unification Church. It is known that God has carried out the providence of restoration while holding this term in His inner heart, wishing for its realization. 

When God created Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden and blessed them, He also hoped for that blessing to be realized. Yet, no one has been able to realize that blessing until now. We come to understand that God has longed for the realization of the blessing as His greatest desire while enduring a sorrowful position throughout the historical process. 

After going through this 4,000-year historical process, God sent Jesus to this earth to finally carry out the blessing He had originally wanted to give. Although God carried out such a providential history, we know that Jesus also could not reach the position of that blessing and passed away. Even after that, throughout thousands of years of Christian history, many Christians have shed their blood as martyrs, yet we know that they have not been able to fulfill God's desire. 

Therefore, we must understand that the term blessing did not begin with our Unification Church but has been a wish of God that He has pursued and hoped for throughout the historical process since the fall in Genesis. 

God has walked the path of suffering to find a day of that wish, but He has not yet found that day. Thus, if we find that day, it will be a day when historical restoration can take place and a day when God's historical desires can be fulfilled. Considering this, we must recognize how immense the position of the blessing is. 

Fallen humanity was not born with a direct blood relationship centered on God. Therefore, unless we deny this and establish a new relationship with God to return to our original position, we cannot enter the position of blessing. In other words, because we were born in the world of fallen death, we must be resurrected to return to the world of life centered on God. We must be reborn. 

However, being born is not the end; we must go through a process of growth. To do this, we must establish various conditions for restoration. In establishing these conditions for restoration, we must take responsibility not only for individual missions but also for national and global missions. We must understand that the issue of blessing is determined by how we have carried out these responsibilities. 

When we look at the issue of blessing today, it is not about individuals like Kim or Park being blessed. So, what must a being possess to enter the position of blessing? There are prerequisites that must be met. The blessing is not for the individual alone; it is to enable that individual to form a new family that represents their tribe, nation, and the world. That family is not just for the individual, but it must represent the tribe and nation, and further, it must be a family that can represent the world. We must understand that without forming such a family, the blessing cannot be established. 

The providential history of finding a man and a woman who can be blessed
This is because, although the ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, were two individuals, they stand at a historical starting point, so it does not end with just those two. Through those two, a new family will be manifested, and further, a new tribe, and eventually, a new nation will surely emerge. The place where this global foundation is determined is precisely the place of blessing. 

Because Adam and Eve lost this place of blessing due to the fall, we find ourselves in a position where we must restore it. Therefore, this blessing is not limited to the blessing of our individual selves. Thus, unless we resolve to receive the blessing from a position that can transcend the standards of nation and tribe, we cannot see the completion of restoration. 

From this perspective, we must understand how serious the position of the individual who must enter the place of blessing is. That place is where all the sorrows woven from the past to the present can be resolved, where God's desires that have not yet been fulfilled can start anew, and where a new future can begin. 

So, what has the 6,000-year history been seeking? It has been a history seeking one man. What have countless prophets and ancestors sacrificed for since the family of Adam? What has been the content of their struggles? It has been to find one man, one Adam. After finding that man, what must be done? We must find one woman through that man. Just as God created Adam first and then created Eve through Adam, they have been fighting until now to fulfill their historical responsibility to find Adam. 

Once that Adam is found, what must happen? From that day, Eve must be recreated. The recreation cannot be done in a natural environment. Without completely resolving the victorious decision point that has been established before the nation and the world, the blessing cannot be achieved. 

Who is the one born as God's man to restore all that has failed after Adam? It is Jesus. However, even Jesus cannot fulfill the will alone. No matter how much Jesus inherited all the contents of the providence concerning the nation of Israel, he cannot form a nation by himself. To form a nation, Jesus must first establish a new family. 

To establish a new family, we must find one woman who can represent the countless women on earth. In other words, we must find one woman who can represent many women nationally and globally. To extract that one woman from the world of Satan, we must engage in a battle to cut down the many Satans who have opposed and rebelled throughout history. Unless someone joins in this and stands against Satan to find one woman, we cannot retrieve Eve from the world of Satan. 

In other words, unless we present victorious conditions that can completely surpass all that has been invaded by Satan for 4,000 years, we cannot find Eve, who has been lost in the world of Satan. Therefore, this is not a simple matter. 

Thus, to become a historical woman, one must resolve the contents that have historically failed. Furthermore, to become a woman of the era, one must establish a standard that has fulfilled the duty of loyalty and filial piety before heaven, representing all women of the era. And as one woman, she must approach one man with the heart of a virtuous woman. 

Without such a woman appearing, we cannot find the restored Eve that has been hoped for throughout history. In other words, we cannot establish a substantial being that can represent all women in history. Therefore, creating the environment to find that one woman is not a simple issue. Since that position is one-on-one, we must recognize that it contains historical significance. 

When we find that one woman, a new nation will be formed through her, and a new world will be established through that one woman. Considering this fact, we must understand that bringing about the result of recreation by finding that one woman is not an easy task.

**The Internal Sorrow of Heaven**

We are living while experiencing that sorrow permeates every aspect of our lives. We come to realize that there are many direct and indirect driving forces that can launch us toward new goals through that sorrow. 

**Israel as a Nation Motivated by Sorrow**

Looking at history, among oppressed nations, those with a clear purpose have not perished even as their period of oppression has lengthened; rather, they have become more united. We can glimpse this fact through history.

Wherever they went, persecution and sorrow always greeted them, but they used that sorrow to set a standard for hope. Thus, sorrow can be a condition for despair, but for those who have a purpose, it can become a condition that forms the inner strength to fulfill that purpose. 

So what did the Israelite people long for? They longed to stand within the ideological realm where the nation and people are united in heart centered on the one God. **Order of Service Among Blessed Families**
<Summary of the Message> Each family should unite and strive competitively to set an example for one another while thoroughly serving the higher families. Higher families can criticize lower families, but lower families must not criticize higher families. From now on, we must establish the tradition of the family. The 36 families should not think they are superior and act in ways that violate etiquette and damage dignity and face.

You should not take more than three days to visit the teacher while you are in Seoul. If the 36 families are the district leaders, then the 72 families and 124 families in that district must report everything to the district leader. There, the 36 families must play the role of parents.

If you violate what was decided at the association's general meeting, there may be a way to be forgiven, but if you violate what was firmly decided at the family meeting, there is no remedy.

The Unification Church is a family church centered on the unified tribe. In the future, the church must be a church centered on our home, and that nation must also be a nation centered on our home. The center of the 36 families is not the Adam family or the Noah family, but the Jacob family.

We must organize the internal environment of the family regarding the will. Even when evangelizing, do not do it alone; set the condition that you always did it with your wife, and that your sons and daughters also participated.

April 4, 1970 (Saturday), Unification Industry Dormitory Auditorium.
* This message was given during a district leader meeting and is compiled from the report published in issue 18.

Daily life in the family embodies the principle of correct division and cooperation. That is, even when parting in the morning for each other's work, part joyfully, and when meeting again in the evening, meet joyfully. When returning home, discuss and share the events of the day with your spouse and children, correcting any mistakes. The whole family must be connected with love and laughter.

Discuss the will between husband and wife, but what is said beyond that should not be spoken outside and must remain a secret. They must be a couple who can keep such secrets. Until now, couples in the world have not been able to do this.

Children should say, "I love my dad! I love my mom! I am so happy to see that mom and dad love each other." Such a family is a resting place for children. It should become a foundation of eternal joy and pride that they do not want to leave for any other place. In such a family, can there be fights?

You must always think that the three-stage foundation is cooperating behind your activities. If you think that God is cooperating, that your wife is cooperating, and that your children are cooperating, victory is certain. Move forward with this self-awareness.

Blessed families must be examples both inside and out. Men should unite under the goal of the church's operation, and women should unite under the goal of the business field. Pray a lot. If you pray a lot, you will never feel lonely even if you live alone. Prayer is like breathing. If you pray a lot, you will become spiritually bright. You will also become quite sensitive and gain discernment between good and evil. Prayer involves sacrifice and sincerity.

Ministers should dedicate one-tenth of their time to God. After that, they should work for their families and the country. One-third of their time should be spent working for their family, country, and God. And they should pray at least 2 hours and 24 minutes a day. It is best if two-thirds of that prayer is done in the early morning.

The reason we have gathered in this place this morning is not to meet anyone else. We have gathered according to the connection with the Father, to receive the mission and responsibility you bestow upon us. May your high and precious holiness protect us, and may this environment be completely encompassed within your authority. Please let us feel that we can reflect your holiness and overcome ourselves. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.

Many people have called upon you, and many children have walked the path of restoration, but we realize that we have not yet achieved the victory you desired, and we have not left a path to be grateful for on the path of restoration.

Now we stand on this path of restoration, calling upon the Father, and we must know that this inevitable path we must take is to work only for the Father, rely only on the Father, and restore the relationships around us.

As loneliness increases, let us not sigh in the place where we cannot escape the bonds of sorrow. To escape this, we must call upon the Father. We must establish a connection with the Father.

We know that our path must be one where we must establish a deeper connection with the Father, so let us be your children who have come here today, longing for and admiring the Father. Let us be your children who can admire the Father to the extent that we can immerse ourselves in our longing and desire to see him.

Please let this hour be one where the Father can come before us, give us commands, and comfort us. If there are any shortcomings in ourselves, let us reveal them before the Father and, if there are any aspects of ourselves that are not suitable in the past, present, or future, let us criticize ourselves once again. Thus, let us become those who pledge victory in the battle against Satan, aligned with your holiness. Let us run toward the battlefield of the future, knowing that we can be the sons and daughters whom the Father can hope for and command.

Are there groups here who are praying while longing for this place? Are there many of your children who are longing for this place and hoping for the Father’s grace? I earnestly hope and wish that you will bless them a thousandfold and ten thousandfold, so that they may remain until the last day.

Please remember your children scattered around the world. I earnestly hope and wish that you will be with those who call Korea their homeland and the nation of hope. Furthermore, centered on Korea and Japan, we are approaching a critical mission and responsibility in Asia. I also know that a battle to determine life and death is currently being fought through the Japanese members, so Father, I earnestly hope you will be with them in that place.

They are lonely groups. For the sake of Korea, which no one sympathizes with, they have stepped forward for this nation and this people. I earnestly hope and wish that you will look upon those who march toward the enemy’s camp with bare bodies and show them mercy.

What they desire is not just their own desire. They are a pitiful group carrying the will left by the Father for humanity, so I know that the Father will surely be with them in that place. I earnestly hope and wish that the Father will raise a new form of flag in that place, and I earnestly request that your will be manifested through the environment in which they move.

Father, please watch over the path of Korea. May this people be able to fulfill the mission entrusted to them, take on their respective responsibilities, and inherit the connection with the True Parents. Furthermore, may this people be one that can stand before the Father, lacking nothing in preparing the form of a nation before many nations, and be a people worthy of your love. I earnestly request and wish for this.

Father, tomorrow is Parents' Day. I know that some members in Japan will come here today, so I earnestly hope that through all the stories exchanged, we can boast of the Father and solidify our connection with him.

I earnestly hope that the various issues arising in April will progress under your protection and according to your will. During the remaining period, may we leave only results that please you, and may we be able to draw even one step closer to the Father during this short time.
I humbly ask for Your protection and guidance, and I have conveyed all these words in reverence to the Holy Name of the True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> In the lives of us humans, there are various paths. There are paths taken for oneself, for one's family, for one's country, and for the world, among others. Most people wish to walk the path for themselves and for their own side. There are not many who live for others.  
The path Jesus had to take  
When we reflect on the course of history, we can see that those who lived for others generally became historical figures. Of course, among them, there will be those who remained on God's side and those who remained on the side of the enemy. From this perspective, our Unification Church must go the path for the enemy rather than for our own side first. Only then can we reach the destination of the path we must take.  
The Bible states, "A man's enemies will be the members of his own household." (Matthew 10:36) We know well that as long as that enemy remains an eternal enemy, that religion cannot reach the final path it must take.  
The inevitable course Jesus had to take upon coming to this earth was to first walk the path that the nation must take, and then the path that the world and humanity must take through countless historical processes. However, does that mean that the path Jesus himself had to take was all finished? No, it is necessary to also go through the path that the enemies must take.  
Because Jesus had to walk such a path, even until the last moment of His death on the cross, He prayed for the enemies, saying, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they are doing." (Luke 23:34) Jesus could not help but pray in this way because there was an inevitable path of destiny that He had to walk.  
Israel is a name obtained through Jacob. It is a noun given because Jacob won the battle that arose from seizing Esau's blessing. If he had not won, it would have been a sorrowful thing for God. Why? Because the term Israel symbolically carries different meanings. Within the word Israel is the content that not only Jacob himself won, but also that Jesus would be placed in a position to win. This is how the name Israel first appeared.  
Considering this fact, just as the individual of Israel went through such a position, the family of Israel must also be in a position where it cannot avoid going through such a path. Furthermore, the nation of Israel and the state of Israel must also go through such a path, and the rulers who must lead the nation of Israel are also in a position where they must go through that path of destiny. Therefore, Jesus, as the representative leader who came to rule Israel, had to walk the path of destiny on behalf of the individuals, tribes, nations, and states of Israel.  
To establish the realm of Israel does not mean to establish authority limited to ruling only the nation of Israel. Therefore, we must understand that the path Jesus had to walk was to also establish authority beyond the nation of Israel.  
This is also true for God, who must advance the providence with the premise of restoration. God does not walk the path of restoration centered only on His love; rather, when a person on God's side is formed to a certain standard, that standard must be used to restore individuals, families, and so on in the world of enemies. In other words, after establishing a foundation for victory centered on one's own side, one must also apply the authority of victory to the world of enemies, which is the path that religion must take. You must understand this.  
Until now, in the process of walking the path of restoration, God has unfolded His will for the side of heaven, but the ultimate result cannot be possessed by the side of heaven alone. There must be a standard to subdue the enemy side, and without having a standard that can unite around that enemy side, you cannot fulfill the will you desire.  
The path of restoration seen through the providence of Cain and Abel  
This begins from Abel of the Adam family. However, although God called Abel to stand, it is not that he can only go centered on Abel. Abel must first go ahead on the path he must take and seek the path that Cain must take. To seek the path that Cain must take, Abel himself must stand in a subjective position before Cain.  
So, how does Abel stand in a subjective position? He must achieve a certain limited purpose. This is because only when he stands in a position where he has fulfilled his own responsibility can he represent the central position. And at some boundary point of his own path, that is, when it comes to the boundary of the individual, he must not start again centered on the family, but must elevate Cain, who is in a conflicting position in the world of enemies, to the same position as himself. You must understand that if Abel does not unite with Cain here, Abel's path will be blocked.  
In a family, there are parents, and there are siblings centered around those parents. Therefore, to move toward a happy family, Abel cannot go alone. This is the path of restoration. Even if Abel establishes a standard of a family that can serve the parents, he cannot return to the parents without addressing Cain. Only in the place where Cain and Abel are united can they meet the parents, and only then can the parents be restored and finally reach their destination. This is the teaching of the principle.  
This destiny applies not only to Abel but also to Noah. When viewed through Noah, there was a path that Noah, centered on the people, had to take as an individual, and we know that he worked hard for 120 years to go through this individual course. Noah had the responsibility to elevate his own family on the foundation of this hard work. To elevate it to the standard that God desires, there must be internal and external unity. If Noah went from the internal position, then from the external position, the family must go, and a standard must be established where the individual and the family can be said to have united. Only then can the family itself be saved.  
Abraham is the same. Abraham cannot go alone either. He must take with him the children belonging to him or the contents of all things and go to Egypt or any other place, but he must go through a position where the internal and external are united. This is an inevitable course in going the path of restoration that must restore from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world.  
Now, when we look at our Unification Church today, what is the path that the Unification Church must take, the path that remains as an inevitable destiny? If the Unification Church has a path to walk for this country and this nation, and if that path is only toward the side of heaven, it could easily end. However, even if we have walked the path we must walk, it does not end there; we must return to the starting point from which we began and lead those who have become our enemies. This is the path that the Unification Church must take today, and you must understand this.  
From this perspective, in order for us to walk the path of restoration today, we must first establish an expectation of faith as stated in the principle. The expectation of faith is necessary to establish a solid foundation on which one can stand in a subjective position. After that, even if one has become oneself who can go toward the purpose, that alone is not enough; one must return and establish an expectation of substance.
