From this perspective, we can infer that since the 1970s, it has become a time when our Unification Church can revive in every aspect, both internally and externally. Just because we have become materially prosperous does not mean that a leader who uses that material for the Unification Church is a true leader. Furthermore, even if a member of the Unification Church wishes to do so, that person is not a member of the Unification Church.

Unification Church members should use all their possessions for the development of the Unification Church rather than for the development of the established churches. That is how it is used for the Unification Church. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”

When used in that way, it can become ours, but if not, we will lose even what we have. On that day, one will lose their own religion and their own nation. You must understand this.

Then what must the teacher do in the future? Until now, I have worked for you. Now, we have reached a certain limit. It is time for you to take responsibility and move forward. Until now, it has been a time of coming out against the enemy. It has been a time of fighting. But now, it is like a ceasefire. Now it is time for you to go on your own.

The mission of the Unification Church is not just the mission of the teacher. It is your mission, and you must take on that mission. Thus, you must appear as Abel yourselves. Until now, I have been engaged in a war of attrition from the Abel position to lay this foundation. If I have finally stood on a victorious foundation from the Abel position, you must inherit the Abel position centered on the teacher and work to subjugate the established churches. Only then will the time come to resolve the resentment of the Unification Church, just as Cain and Abel had to resolve the resentment of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden. You must understand that this is the inevitable path the Unification Church must take.

Therefore, in the future, when we have something, we cannot use it for ourselves if we want to quickly restore the world. When we work from a position that only serves ourselves, we must return and go again. So what should we do? We must use it for Cain. We must go out with the conviction to work for Cain. Therefore, we must work for the Republic of Korea. The Republic of Korea stands before us as the second Cain position. The first Cain is the established church.

Looking at the time of Jesus, Jesus came to take responsibility for the new Christianity, so Judaism was in the Cain position before Jesus. Jesus had to subjugate Judaism and lead it as one. When completely united, it would lead with something new. That is where the new world, the new Christianity, should have started. Because it did not happen, we must restore this today.

From this perspective, when we look at the Unification Church and the established church, the established church stands in the same position as Judaism in the time of Jesus, while the Unification Church stands in the same position as the new religion that Jesus sought to establish. If Jesus becomes isolated, He will perish. Isn’t that why He bore the cross? In the same way, if our Unification Church becomes isolated, it will perish. It will not fulfill its purpose.

Carry the double cross
Therefore, now that we have elevated the Unification Church to an Abel-type denomination, the issue is how to subjugate the established churches. The Unification Church and the established churches are in an internal and external relationship. What do the established church members in the external position seek? They seek to eat, wear, and sleep centered on people. In other words, they are in a position that emphasizes external issues like food, clothing, and shelter.

To resolve this issue, we only need to do a little better. When there is something good, a fight breaks out when someone claims it for themselves. Even if placed in a position of servitude in the enemy's world, one must gain credit and praise from the master. To do this, when there is food, one must give it to the enemy even if they do not eat it themselves. Although they may outwardly dislike it and criticize it, they will be moved internally.

They will think, “That guy is someone I can trust.” When good food is available, I must give it to Cain instead of eating it myself, and when I have good clothes, I must dress Cain first. When I can go to a good place, I must yield for Cain. If we carry out such strategies, subjugating Cain will be simple.

The strategy Jacob used to subjugate Esau is exactly that. Jacob presented everything he could eat and wear before Esau, saying, “All of this is for you, brother. Everything I have gained through decades of struggle in suffering is for you. I will give you everything, whether it is servants, flocks, or children. Please welcome me as a new brother centered on love, clearing up the past enmity between us.”

When this happens, not only will he find his brother, but he will also find his sister. By finding his brother, he finds his brother’s family, and everything his brother possesses becomes his own. In other words, everything becomes the property of Isaac’s family centered on Isaac. You must understand that God carries out such strategies.

From this perspective, Christianity has contributed to the establishment of a new cultural world globally after enduring suffering and adversity for 2,000 years. In that regard, Christians are historical benefactors. Therefore, even if Christianity made mistakes at one time, we should not whip it to make amends but should embrace it with love and recreate the standard that God hoped for and expected. You must understand that this is the path the Unification Church must take.

Therefore, in the future, we must unite with the established churches, and then we must unite with the Republic of Korea. When the 30 million people arm themselves with the ideology centered on God’s will and unite around the Christian sphere, there will be no problem with North Korea. After we have completely organized ourselves internally and externally, we must fight against Kim Il-sung with words. The final issue that must be resolved openly remains. There will come a time when Kim Il-sung will have no choice but to shake hands. The global situation will unfold that way. In other words, there will come a time when he cannot refuse to yield his position. The communists will remain in this world until then.

In this way, centered on the Republic of Korea, the Cain and Abel nations will finally become one. Only then can the Abel nation, which has the form of a sovereign state centered on the Unification Church, that is, the Republic of Korea, embark on a journey toward the world. You must understand that the time is approaching when this will happen. Therefore, you must clearly know the path Abel must take and bear the double cross.

Until now, you have fought centered on your will and have engaged in pioneering efforts, but that path is also the path you must take in the future. You must go and prepare everything. You must stand in the same position as Jacob. Therefore, the question is how to leave behind the results that can be said to have been done for Esau. You must understand that this is the path that can determine the fate of the world and this nation. You must know that this is the inevitable path we must take and pray from this perspective.

Move with subjective and proactive authority
Therefore, we must be grateful that Christianity in Korea opposes us and that this Republic of Korea is divided into North and South. We should be thankful because we are in a position to restore and indemnify centered on our kin.

You must understand this and dedicate special devotion for six months from May to October in 1970. We must pray specially. This is not to destroy North Korea but to seek a way for North Korea to surrender before Heaven. To do this, we must first pray for the established churches. Next, we must pray for the Republic of Korea. The Unification Church must have the subjective and proactive authority to digest the established churches, South Korea, and North Korea and must move forward.

To do this, we must carry out a siege operation. We must connect the three nations. Looking at Korea, North and South are facing each other, but internally, the standards that the Unification Church is advancing are directly opposed to what North Korea is currently presenting. When looking at the Soviet Union, China, and North Korea, Korea is isolated. Restoration cannot happen with Adam alone. Restoration must connect from Adam to Eve, and from Eve to the archangel.

Korea is the Adam nation, Japan is the Eve nation, and China is the archangel nation. From this perspective, it is faster to restore among Asians than to involve Westerners in the restoration process. From this perspective, we must love Cain.

Just as the Unification Church calls True Parents, in the world of Satan, North Korea also calls Kim Il-sung “father.” It is a relative relationship. The side of Satan is connected through the Soviet Union to China and then to North Korea, while the side of Heaven is connected through Korea to Japan and Free China. When we create a connection point in Asia, communism will decline.

From a principled perspective, when the sovereign is changed three times, good times will come before our will. The path we must take is not just for Korea. It is a path that must take responsibility for the world through North Korea. Because we must bear this dual responsibility, it cannot be easy, and we cannot be idle.

You must know that you are in a position where you cannot avoid carrying the double cross, and as you walk this path, you must gladly accept all hardships and adversities, becoming those who take responsibility for the nation and all humanity. You must walk this path while growing your capabilities in your current life and praying with all your heart. As you face the 1970s, you must not become a dropout in walking this painful path to lay a solid foundation. I ask that you become that way.

Our Resolution as We Enter the 1970s
<Word> Today, as you all know, is the 11th Parents' Day. We have held this commemorative ceremony several times. While we let the Parents' Day pass as just a day of celebration in the 1960s, this new 70s must be a newly welcomed Parents' Day. 
The history of restoration has been a history to establish one person. 
Since the fall of humanity, God has longed for Parents' Day throughout the providential course, but that day had not come. However, today, our Unification Church has appeared and has finally established this Parents' Day. We know well that with the establishment of this Parents' Day, the Day of Children, the Day of All Things, and the Day of God have also been established. 
We know that until the establishment of this Parents' Day in 1960, all created beings existing in heaven and on earth have been tracing the history of sorrow according to the principle of indemnity and restoration. 
After the fall of Adam and Eve, God has fought for 4,000 years, going through the time of Noah, the time of Abraham, and the time of Moses, with a heart that no one can fathom, to restore this Parents' Day. We must understand this fact. 
God has sent many prophets and sages to this earth, establishing a chosen people from individuals to families, tribes, nations, and preparing a foundation that could become the center of that chosen people until the coming of Jesus. 
In light of this fact, that 4,000-year history was a history to establish just one person, Jesus. 
From this providential perspective, the people of that time had to unite with Jesus. However, we know that the chosen Israelite nation at that time could not unite with Jesus. 
Can the fallen descendants of Adam simply be connected to the original parents? There must be a form of individuals, families, tribes, nations, and states so that they can stand in the position of the nation, tribe, family, and true individual that Jesus desires, aligning with the heart of Jesus. Only then can Jesus establish himself on the foundation prepared through history. 
We understand this through the principles. 
For an individual to stand in such a position, the family must support them, and for the family to stand, the tribe must support them, and for the tribe to stand, the nation must support them, and for the nation to stand, the world must support them. The Israelite nation that Jesus came to had to walk a heavy path of indemnity. We know this. 
Therefore, for Jesus to stand, the family of Joseph had to be a protective fence. For the family of Joseph to stand, the tribe of Joseph had to be a protective fence, and for the tribe of Joseph to stand, the entire Israelite nation had to unite and become a protective fence. In other words, all of this must be unified internally and externally on the foundation of one center, so that Jesus can carry out the new history of the gospel. 
It should have been so, but Jesus did not receive love from his family. Because he lacked that protective fence, he had to walk a sorrowful three years of public life. 
What is God's sorrow? God has worked for 4,000 years to send just one Jesus, establishing one family, but that established family could not become the protective fence for Jesus. In other words, although that family was established to protect only Jesus, because that family stood in a position of division from Jesus, he had to walk the path of suffering alone. This fact must have been an unspeakable shock to God, who had hoped for 4,000 years. We must understand this. 
The family of Joseph was established in such a hopeful position before God, but that family failed to fulfill its responsibility. The family of Joseph was prepared on the foundation of the 4,000-year history of the Israelite nation to stand in the position of representing that nation. To do that, God had to connect relatives to the heavenly side centered around that family. To connect those relatives, John the Baptist was born. Through him, it was prepared for Jesus, the Messiah, to come. 
Despite being in a position to absorb the tribe centered around that connection, the family of Joseph failed to take responsibility and could not absorb that tribe. As a result, Jesus faced national and ethnic calamities, losing his family, tribe, nation, and state, and found himself in a position where he had to postpone all the purposes he had to fulfill on this earth and bear the cross. We must reflect on this situation of Jesus once again. 
What was Jesus supposed to do when he came to this earth? He was to establish Parents' Day, establish Children’s Day, establish the Day of All Things, and establish God’s Day. However, no one understood that Jesus came with such an immense historical mission. Not even his loving parents understood, nor did the twelve disciples who followed him. 
In this position, Jesus was in deep contemplation about how to fulfill the mission and responsibility given to him by God. The path he took from the Mount of Olives to Calvary was exceedingly miserable and despairing. 
Even in such a position, Jesus left behind a new hope, saying, "I will come again; you must wait for that day." He also promised that when he comes again, he will come as a bridegroom, and that they should prepare themselves as brides to wait for that time. We understand that this was Jesus' final testament as he left this earth. 
Christianity, which followed this testament, has woven a miserable history. Because the first Israel could not stand before God's will, Christianity, which stands in the position of the second Israel, has taken on the responsibility of the world to lay a global foundation. We understand this as the history of Christianity. 
Because Jesus had to die, the history of Christianity, which should have led to blessings, had to pay the price of blood. Without this, it could not develop from individuals to families, from families to tribes, from tribes to nations, and from nations to the world. Because Jesus shed his blood on the cross, Christianity has connected the blood of martyrs wherever it has gone, leading to global development. 
Now, Christianity has undeniably become a global religion. What is the single issue that Christianity must address, which God requires? It is to prepare as a bride. Of course, the whole world must prepare as a bride, but a specific nation, a specific people, a specific family, and a specific individual must prepare as a bride for the bridegroom who is coming. This is the mission that Christianity must fulfill to welcome the Lord who is coming and the preparation that must be made on this earth. 
God has developed Christianity through a history of sorrow that no one knows, in order to prepare for the end times, to welcome the day of the Lord's return. He has established a specific nation and a specific organization that believe in Christianity to carry out the history of preparing as a bride. 
We must understand this fact. 
Today, what must Korea inherit to occupy the realm of the third Israel? It is not merely about inheriting the external traditions of Christianity; it is about inheriting the internal traditions of Christianity. So what is the internal tradition of Christianity? It is to inherit the inner heart of Jesus, who was expelled from the Israelite nation and died on the cross. If there are no true sons and daughters among this nation who can do so, Korea cannot occupy the realm of the third Israel. 
Therefore, from the day God extended his hand of providence for salvation centered on Korean Christianity, he has developed the external traditions that allow this nation to inherit the history of Christianity. At the same time, without anyone knowing, God has raised many individuals and many organizations to prepare internally to inherit this internal tradition. 
Thus, God raised the Cheolsan New Church centered around Kim Seong-do, the Bokjung Church centered around Heo Ho-bin, and Pastor Lee Yong-do. They have been preparing for the time of the Lord's return centered around the year 1945. We only come to know the fact that many organizations and individuals were prepared for that day after going through history. 
At that time, it was a historical environment where no one could guarantee who would take on the ultimate mission to fulfill God's will. In such circumstances, many spiritual people fought to take on the internal responsibilities of Christianity while facing persecution and opposition from all people. However, now when we reflect on it, we see that all those who fought at that time have disappeared. This struggle has continued from specific pastor classes to elder classes and down to layperson classes. 
The specific pastors who took on responsibilities at that time had to be connected to external Christianity. If the internal spiritual history and external Christianity had united, a heavenly path centered on the nation and state could have started from there. However, all the pastors who were responsible for external Christianity and those who were taking on internal responsibilities failed to discern and understand God's will.
Unable to fulfill the mission entrusted to them by the times, they began to doubt their own calling when they faced misunderstanding and jealousy from the environment of that era. Consequently, because they failed to carry out the responsibilities given to them by God, these responsibilities were passed down to the elders or deacons. 

Reflecting on the sorrows of such history, we can see that now is the time for laypeople to embrace God. This is something we must understand. In other words, Christianity has gradually fallen from a central position that could unify and lead the whole, to a more flat and fragmented stance. 

If we look at this from the perspective of today's external world, it is similar to the transition from totalitarian states to democratic states. Therefore, we have now entered an era that emphasizes faith centered on the individual. 

For this reason, we must connect the worldview centered on the individual in the external world with the individual-centered view of heaven in Christianity. Thus, we must restore the individual, the family, the nation, and the world. The one who bears the overall responsibility and mission for this is the Lord of the Second Advent, and you must understand that this is the mission of the Lord of the Second Advent. 

In the present age, whether internal or external, every nation, every people, every tribe, and every family is in a time that disperses everything, focusing on the individual. In both external life and internal faith, it is an era where individuals maintain the lifeblood of their existence. Therefore, we must recognize that current democracy and established churches must transcend this era. 

Who can fulfill the new history that will remain for future generations centered on this individualistic faith? What kind of group is this? It is a person with a new view of family, a new view of tribe, a new view of nation, and a new view of the world from the perspective of the individual. Now, within the Christian realm centered on God, there must emerge individuals who can present a new view of family, tribe, nation, world, and heaven to the world. Such a new Christian movement must unfold on this earth. Thus, you must understand that we are moving into a new era.

As a result, he ended up serving as a slave in Potiphar's house and later was imprisoned. However, even in such a position, God protected him. God raised him to the position of prime minister of that nation, prepared to die for his people. After Joseph became the prime minister of Egypt, his eleven brothers were restored, and only then was he able to serve his parents.

Wasn't this a fact that empirically demonstrated the overall circumstances of the historical age?

So, what position does our Unification Church occupy today? It is in a fate similar to that of Joseph. Numerous denominations have tried to sell out the Unification Church. Moreover, they have not only tried to sell us out but also to bury us in a waterless desert. They wished for our death and for us to be devoured by wolves and dogs. However, we did not die. Who would have thought we would come this far without dying?

When those who tried to drive us out face the misfortune of their entire family being destroyed, God will open the way for their revival. Isn't this the current position of the democratic world and the established churches?

What we must understand today is that we should not emulate any nation with a new ideology. You must understand that. Do not envy or imitate America or the American church. That is why the teacher does not have the intention of living in America. To save America in the future, we must not be influenced by America. You must not be influenced by any liberal ideology. You must not be influenced by Japan or any other nation. Rather, they should be influenced by us.

They are people who have lost their subjectivity. That is the current situation. The world is such a world.

We must establish the form of Abel-like individuals, families, tribes, nations, and states before such a world. When we establish such a world, the end times will approach this world. It is certain.

Just as Christianity has established a Christian realm in the external world, the Unification Church has also established a standard through external activities to connect with the nation of the Republic of Korea. So, what is the problem now? First, the issue is for Christianity and the world to become one, and next, for the Unification Church and Christianity to become one. Within the nation, the issue is for the Unification Church and established churches to become one, and in the world, the issue is for the Unification Church and world Christianity to become one. Right now, there is a clear division inside and outside.

What we must do here is to unify the inside and outside in a familial way. The time has come for that. We must completely unify and move forward. For that, the established churches must cooperate. This is the path they must take. The time has come for that.

Next, be an example personally and in your families. Love your nation more than you love the Unification Church. Furthermore, love the world more than you love the Republic of Korea. In that sense, starting from the 1970s, we will ensure that at events, people from at least three nations will participate. Naturally, that will happen. The time has come for that. And today, representatives from three nations are gathered here. Including Korea, that makes four nations. In the future, we will celebrate such days globally.

What does this mean? It means that the time for the providential will to manifest before this world has come. Therefore, we must unite now. We must unite for victory, not for defeat. This is where the term "victorious unification front" comes from. What is at the center of this? It is the family. Therefore, families must unite. That is why we established 430 families.

Since the 36 families, 72 families, and 124 families could not take responsibility, we say that the 430 families should take on what they could not do. That is why we established the 430 families. And we must inspire the senior families. The 124 families, 72 families, and 36 families should be inspired by them. In this way, they should resemble the 430 families. Will they resemble them or not? "We will resemble them." Then, you must go through hardships.

The teacher has spoken to you today about how important the unification of families is and how busy this era is. Now, if families unite and surpass the third seven-year course, the world will submit to us. Reflecting on how we surpassed the three-year course of the first seven-year course, you must go out for three years of witnessing centered on the standard of being one with the teacher's family until 1972. If I say this, you might think, "Back then, they said three years would be enough, and now it's three years again," but the situation is different from then. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

The inside and outside must unite as one for the three-year course. Just as there was a three-year period of sacrificial conditions for personal victory, we must go through a three-year course as families. Your family and the teacher's family must become one, enduring the three-year period until 1972 as if they are one body inside and outside. Thus, we aim to save this nation, this people, and the world.

What the teacher has said will undoubtedly be correct. How happy we are to have entered this historical realm! This is a dream-like story. While it may seem like a dream to you, it is indeed a reality. When the inside and outside families become one, and we unite with the established churches, the Republic of Korea will easily be restored. Now is the second period of economic growth for our country, and if we unite ideologically, economic growth will not be a problem. Moreover, if the 600,000 national troops and 2.5 million local reserve forces are armed with the ideology of unification, Kim Il-sung will not be a problem. It will not be a problem at all. When this happens, the Unification Church, in the Abel position, and the established church, in the Cain position, will unite to form an internal foundation, becoming one with the nation in the external position. Furthermore, the Republic of Korea will become the internal nation, and North Korea will become the external nation. That is why the issue is from now on.

The first unification is for the established church and us to become one, the second unification is for the unified Christian realm and the Republic of Korea to become one, and the third unification is for South Korea and North Korea to become one. Once this is achieved, the world will inevitably be drawn to us.

This is the path we must take from now on. This is the path that lies ahead of our families. Until now, we have been dealing with this nation, but now we have entered an era where we can deal with the world. We just need to execute our strategy well. In preparation for that, the teacher has been developing strategies inside and outside to push forward. The world will undoubtedly collapse. It is bound to collapse. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Go the way that serves Cain until the end. 

For whom do you exist? Not for yourselves. For whom then? "For Cain." It is for Cain. We exist for those who wished for our downfall, for our enemies. Who did Joseph serve in the world of enemies? He served the eleven brothers who tried to kill him. Since losing brothers in the world of enemies is neither humanity's will nor God's will, we must find them again. Therefore, the Unification Church must shed tears and pray for the established church. We must devote ourselves for them. Do you understand? "Yes."

Starting from 1968, a new fortune will return to Christianity. Our era is coming. A new emerging denomination will appear with the form of religion, and it will be filled with the grace of God. That is the current situation. The question is how to connect this radically to established Christianity. For this purpose, the teacher has been operating behind the scenes until now, without your knowledge. We have entered the realm of possibility.

When we consider how to establish the Republic of Korea before the will, we are not unhappy. What if the denominations of Cain and Abel had become Christianity and Buddhism? How difficult would that be? If Christianity and Buddhism had been connected to the restoration issue from the perspective of Cain and Abel, how resentful and difficult would that have been? Would that have been easy or difficult? "Difficult." Knowing all this, we realize that all of this was God's love. The established church and the Unification Church are one brother. Considering this, the fact that the Unification Church has walked the path of suffering is not unjust. We must recognize that God's love is present in that.

Although the established church has stood against God in the restoration process, and has taken a position that supports Satan, Satan must ultimately stand in a position that cooperates with God's will. The established church must complete this task in the future. From this perspective, the Unification Church must achieve economic revival. It must be done by any means necessary. It may seem hopeless now, but you just need to get through the three-year hurdle. If all families follow the teacher's guidance, whether to live or die, and endure for three years, you will see whether the teacher's words are true or not. You will see whether the teacher lied or whether our principles are correct.

Now, when you unite, will you only unite above your body, or below? Will you become one while leaving some behind? "We will become one completely." For that, you must unite in a challenging position. You must unite in a place where life and death intersect. Therefore, if the center falls, you must fall together. Your heart and body must be completely united in the same position. If that happens, even at the moment when your heart and body fall and despair, you can receive a new stimulus to rise again. What day will that be? It will be the day when all hope arises inside and outside.

Recently, I heard from a regional leader that he moved seventeen times while serving as a regional leader. After moving seventeen times, he now thinks, "Will I move again?" As a result, his clothes have become so tattered that he cannot show his face. Was that a good thing or a bad thing? It was good, wasn't it? Still, do not die. Even if you fall, do not die. If you die, that is the end. Even if you fall, do not complain.

"O God, let me sleep peacefully," and fall. But that does not mean to die.

When Jacob was in such difficult circumstances, did the angels of heaven go up and down? Do you think they went up and down when he was in a position of confidence and overflowing hope? No, they came when he was at the point of death… when he had nowhere to go and was sleeping on a stone pillow, how miserable was that situation? If it were you, you would think, "Why did I have to go through that?" And then you would try to become a spiritual person in the Unification Church. (Laughter)

Let us create a Parents' Day that all members celebrate with the same heart. 

In a position where everything collapses inside and outside, that is when a new beginning truly occurs, and it indicates that our time is drawing near. You must understand that.

When I say this, someone who is new to the Unification Church might think it would be good to follow the person known as the founder of the Unification Church, but they might think, "Oh! This seems very deceptive." (Laughter)
Hmm) Such a person has misunderstood emotions. In the past, individuals followed their own intentions, but from now on, families must unite and follow together. If the teacher's family goes hungry, your family must feed the teacher's family even if your own family goes hungry. Will you do that or not? "I will." Will you bring it back or not? "I will bring it back." That's good. (Laughter) The issue is not that your family goes hungry. The point is that you must feed the teacher's family. At the same time, you must resolve your own grievances. So, can you die? If you die, the teacher's family will starve to death... (Laughter) That's how it is. Therefore, while it's okay for me to die, you must think that it shouldn't be that way. Then, it means you cannot die. Not only that, but my country will disappear, and my world will disappear. That’s why I want to unite with the teacher for the next three years. Do you understand? "Yes." Then what will you do from now on? You must make it difficult for families for three years. You must make it difficult for families. During these three years, we must celebrate Parents' Day as the best day. Everyone, are you celebrating Parents' Day in 1970 as the best or the worst? Think about it. Is it the best or the worst? "It's the best." You say it's the best? How are you celebrating it now? Is it the best or the worst? "It's the worst." That's right. Now that you know this, for the next Parents' Day in the second year, let's catch about seven cows. Do you understand? "Yes." Let's catch one from each province. 

Everyone, think about it. When you come up here from each district, the district leaders are going to celebrate Parents' Day. I want to see it too, but only the district leaders go, so what does Parents' Day have to do with us! They will be complaining while smacking their lips. How pitiful will they be? That's why we should catch one cow from each district and hold a feast to celebrate this day. Isn't that something we can do? 

So, for next year's Parents' Day, let's catch one cow each. We need to bring one front leg and one back leg. Since there are eight provinces, that makes four cows. Right? With those four cows, let's hold a feast. It's not because the teacher wants to eat, but because it seems like a good idea. 

You might think that on a day like Parents' Day, the teacher would be very comfortable, but I haven't even eaten breakfast yet. I haven't eaten breakfast and I'm doing this, so Parents' Day is a day of hardship. (Laughter) Until now, it has been a day of hardship, so now it must become a comfortable day. 

Go out to find the heavenly family
From this perspective, the three-year course is important. For three years, families must suffer. Do you understand? "Yes." We must unite around the family. The teacher is working hard to save families. What is the teacher willing to die for? Is it for the individual? "No." It should be for the church rather than for the individual. 

Then among you, there may be someone who thinks that rather than the teacher doing something centered on the 36 families, it would be better if the teacher established a church since there is none in our district, and that the teacher's intention is nonsense. However, that person does not understand well. Such a person is someone who wants to serve themselves. We must live for the family rather than for the individual. If we do not live for the family, there will be no lineage. If families do not unite, there will be no lineage. That is why the teacher values the family more than the church. You all need to understand the teacher's intention. That is why I am asking you to evangelize. Will you evangelize or not? "I will." Will you? "Yes." 

Then, to build an apartment, I will bring cement, gravel, and sand, so you must make the bricks and build everything. Can you do that? "Yes." You can treat all 430 families like forced labor on the labor board? "Yes." (Laughter) Isn't that how it should be? If you do that, won't 700 families build your houses? 

If that happens, then the thousands of families that will be blessed afterward will also do the same. Then, the houses for the people of South Korea must be built by people from other countries. That is our way to survive. (Laughter) (Applause) 

Tightening our belts and living as if we are just managing to settle down, we must still make them work. However, there is no other way. If we don't, we will perish. This is the teacher's way and God's way. 

Carrying the cross means to carry it for others. The cross of the family is carried for the lineage, for the nation, and for the country. In the past, no one carried such a cross. Jesus carried the cross not for the nation, but for the individual, for the individual. 

That is why until now, there has been no heavenly family, and there has been no heavenly nation. What he carried was a cross for the individual, but you must carry the cross for the family. Only then can you finally carry the victorious cross for the lineage, the victorious cross for the nation, or the victorious cross for the country and the world. This tremendous mission has been entrusted to you. How will you bear this? We must walk this path with the resolve to endure the way of suffering and the place of blood. This is the path we must take. 

Because this time has come, we mobilized families through 1969 and beyond 1970, telling them to go beyond families and follow the path that Jesus took. That’s why it happened. Do you understand? "Yes." 

So, did you move well or not? "We moved well." Those who moved well will be commemorated by history. At this time, as we face this moment, we have received God's command in our Unification Church, and by preparing ourselves for the path of death that no one desires, South Korea has been able to welcome a new spring day of revival. The reason we went out to pioneer for 40 days in the provinces is something that no one knew about. Until now, mothers and sons and daughters have gone out and cooperated to lay the foundation, so the rest must follow. Do you understand? "Yes." 

The teacher sent families out in the 1960s to pioneer this land, this nation, and this people. Now we are doing this again. So, you must go back to that land where you devoted your sincerity at that time. 

Just as God's work began on the foundation where Israel devoted its sincerity, the history of the Second Coming of Jesus will also begin on the foundation of sincerity. This is the heavenly tradition. It is the same in our Unification Church, so you must go back to the places where you devoted your sincerity in the 1960s. You must go back and restore it. The tears shed for that district, that neighborhood must not be in vain. The tears of sorrow sown must be reaped as tears of joy. Without that, we cannot save the country. 

You have walked the path of suffering and trials, going through the individual indemnity course. Now you must come to find a new family after the indemnity course. Then, because a foundation of joy will be laid to welcome the new Messiah's family in that town, that town will surely be restored. 

That is why the teacher is pushing you centered on the three-year course. Knowing that you are in such a fate, you must take this time on Parents' Day today to resolve to endure the three-year course. We have not been able to celebrate this Parents' Day as a joyful and thankful day, and this place has not become a proud sight for heaven and earth to watch over, but by making this resolution, you can illuminate this place, so I hope you will make a new determination. Do you understand? "Yes." I hope that will be the case, and those who will do so, let us raise our hands and swear. 

<Prayer> Father, history has been a sad and painful history. I know that many people have been mobilized through such historical days to reach this moment today. Of course, all Unification Church members have been mobilized, but the entire nation and people have also been mobilized to oppose us. This is not only the case in Korea but has been connected globally. 

I am grateful when I think that this has come about not for the desires of any individual, but through your providence centered on heavenly relationships. 

Father, today is the first Parents' Day of the 1970s, so please bless this day. Please allow us to be accepted for following you from an unknown position until now. Through your words, we have understood what time it is now. Therefore, allow us to prepare our attitudes and make a new resolution that can illuminate tomorrow, so that we can approach you even more closely. 

We stand on the fateful path that must go toward the enemy's country, and we have the mission to rise above the communist world. Please bless us as we must go beyond the victory front in Korea and head toward the Asian continent. We must establish a flat era and build it up inside and out, discerning and weaving the history of indemnity. In light of this fact, please allow us to clearly understand that the path we must take is the path of historical development. 

We are the heavenly warriors who have stepped forward to be a light for humanity, so please do not allow us to appear before you in a shameful posture. I earnestly hope and wish that we may become your sons and daughters who can fight and win like warriors. Now, please unite the families. I earnestly hope and wish that we may march vigorously to become the families that will remain on the path we must go through. 

We have vowed to fulfill the remaining mission, so please keep it in your heart. 

On this day, may your children scattered across the regions and the world, who admire and revere your will, feel your infinite love wherever they are. I earnestly ask that your protection and compassionate heart may govern that environment. 

It is April 1970. In this month, we have entrusted all of humanity to you, and we have vowed to make a new start this month, so please allow us to grow and prosper within your will, and grant us success in all matters. I earnestly ask and wish that you personally oversee all subsequent times and procedures. Thank you for everything, and I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen. *
